  "document_summary": "This issue of the Official Gazette of the State of Kuwait, \"Kuwait Today,\" primarily dated September 14, 2025, presents a comprehensive overview of governmental activities. It includes various decrees from the Council of Ministers and several ministries, covering topics such as ambassadorial appointments, nationality withdrawals, and the dissolution of numerous associations. A significant portion details administrative decisions and tender announcements from public authorities and ministries across sectors like public works, health, industry, and financial services. The gazette also features legal notices, including public auctions for properties and vehicles, company liquidations, commercial agency registrations, and bankruptcy proceedings, alongside financial statements from the Central Bank of Kuwait. Notably, it contains Decree-Law No. 134 of 2025, which regulates the use and protection of Red Crescent and Red Cross emblems, reflecting Kuwait's commitment to international humanitarian law.",

Issued on 11 December 1954
Kuwait
The Official Gazette of the Government of the State of Kuwait
Issued by the Ministry of Information / Wizarat Al-I'lam <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>
Department of Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>كويت اليوم</orig> Official Gazette

Issue No. 1756
Seventy-First Year

Sunday
22 Rabi' Al-Awwal 1447 AH
14 September 2025 AD
</header>
# Contents of the Issue

*   **Part Ten (Industrial Designs)**
# Council of Ministers / Majlis Al-Wuzara <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>
## Decree No. 180 of 2025
### Concerning the Repeal of Decree No. 308 of 2006 Establishing the National Center for Educational Development / Al-Markaz Al-Watani li-Tatweer Al-Ta'lim <orig>المركز الوطني لتطوير التعليم</orig>

*   Having reviewed the Constitution,
*   And Amiri Order issued on 2 Dhu al-Qa'dah 1445 AH corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
*   And Decree-Law No. 15 of 1979 concerning Civil Service, and its amending laws,
*   And Decree-Law No. 4 of 1987 concerning Public Education,
*   And Decree issued on 8 Safar 1399 AH corresponding to 7 January 1979 AD concerning the Ministry of Education / Wizarat Al-Tarbiya <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>,
*   And Decree issued on 7 Jumada Al-Awwal 1399 AH corresponding to 4 April 1979 AD concerning the Civil Service System, and its amending decrees,
*   And Decree No. 308 of 2006 establishing the National Center for Educational Development / Al-Markaz Al-Watani li-Tatweer Al-Ta'lim <orig>المركز الوطني لتطوير التعليم</orig>,
*   And based on the submission of the Minister of Education / Wizarat Al-Tarbiya <orig>وزير التربية</orig>,
*   And after the approval of the Council of Ministers / Majlis Al-Wuzara <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>,

We have decreed the following:

### Article One
Decree No. 308 of 2006 referred to above shall be repealed.
<page_end>1</page_end>

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue No. 1756, Seventy-First Year
21
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH – 14/9/2025 AD
</header>


### Article Two
Employees working at the National Center for Educational Development <orig>المركز الوطني لتطوير التعليم</orig> shall be transferred to the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> with their same salaries, grades, allowances, and bonuses.
The competencies, rights, and obligations of the National Center for Educational Development <orig>المركز الوطني لتطوير التعليم</orig> shall be transferred to the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>.

### Article Three
Ministers – each within their respective jurisdiction – shall implement this Decree, which shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> and shall come into force from the date of its publication.

Amir of Kuwait
**Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>**

Prime Minister
**Ahmed Abdullah Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>أحمد عبد الله الأحمد الصباح</orig>**

Minister of Education
**Sayyid Jalal Sayyid Abdul Hassan Al-Tabtabaei <orig>سيد جلال سيد عبد الحسن الطبطبائي</orig>**

Issued at Seif Palace <orig>قصر السيف</orig> on: 15 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 7 September 2025 AD

---

## Decree No. 181 of 2025
### Regarding the Appointment of an Accredited Ambassador

*   Having reviewed the Constitution,
*   And Amiri Order issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
*   And Law No. 21 of 1962 regarding the Diplomatic and Consular Corps System, and its amending laws,
*   And based on the submission of the Minister of Foreign Affairs,
*   And after the approval of the Council of Ministers,

We have decreed the following:

### Article One
Mr. Salem Rashid Al-Shibli <orig>سالم راشد الشبلي</orig> – Ambassador of the State of Kuwait to the Republic of South Africa – shall be appointed, in addition to his current duties, as an accredited Ambassador of the State of Kuwait to the Republic of Mauritius.

### Article Two
The Minister of Foreign Affairs shall implement this Decree, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Amir of Kuwait
**Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>**

Prime Minister
**Ahmed Abdullah Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>أحمد عبد الله الأحمد الصباح</orig>**

Minister of Foreign Affairs
**Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Yahya <orig>عبد الله علي عبد الله اليحيا</orig>**

Issued at Seif Palace <orig>قصر السيف</orig> on: 15 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 7 September 2025 AD
<page_end>2</page_end>

Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 AD
31
</header>

### Article Two
The First Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of Interior <orig>النائب الأول لرئيس مجلس الوزراء ووزير الداخلية</orig> shall implement this Decree, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.
Amir of Kuwait <orig>أمير الكويت</orig>
Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>
First Deputy Prime Minister <orig>النائب الأول لرئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig>
and Minister of Interior <orig>وزير الداخلية</orig>
Fahad Yusuf Saud Al-Sabah <orig>فهد يوسف سعود الصباح</orig>
Issued at Seif Palace <orig>قصر السيف</orig> on: 15 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH corresponding to: 7 September 2025 AD

# Decree No. 184 of 2025
## Regarding the Appointment of an Undersecretary for the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>
- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And Amiri Order <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
- And Decree-Law No. 15 of 1979 regarding Civil Service <orig>الخدمة المدنية</orig>, and its amending laws,
- And the Decree issued on 7 Jumada al-Ula 1399 AH corresponding to 4 April 1979 AD regarding the Civil Service System <orig>نظام الخدمة المدنية</orig>, and its amending decrees,
- And Decree No. 50 of 2017 regarding the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>,
- And based on the submission of the Minister of Social Affairs, Family Affairs, and Childhood <orig>وزير الشئون الاجتماعية وشئون الأسرة والطفولة</orig>,
- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>
We have decreed the following:
### Article One
Dr. Khalid Amer Hamad Al-Ajmi <orig>د. خالد عامر حمد العجمي</orig> is appointed as Undersecretary for the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>.
### Article Two
The Minister of Social Affairs, Family Affairs, and Childhood <orig>وزير الشئون الاجتماعية وشئون الأسرة والطفولة</orig> shall implement this Decree, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.
Amir of Kuwait <orig>أمير الكويت</orig>
Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>
Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig>
Ahmed Abdullah Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>أحمد عبد الله الأحمد الصباح</orig>
Minister of Social Affairs <orig>وزير الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>
and Family Affairs and Childhood <orig>شئون الأسرة والطفولة</orig>
Dr. Amthal Hadi Haif Al-Huwaila <orig>د. أمثال هادي هايف الحويلة</orig>
Issued at Seif Palace <orig>قصر السيف</orig> on: 17 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH corresponding to: 9 September 2025 AD
<page_end>3</page_end>

# Ministry of Information / Wizarat Al-I'lam <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>
## Administrative Decision No. (30) of 2025
Regarding the cancellation of the electronic media outlet license
under the name (Al-Siyaq Al-Barlemani <orig>السياق البرلماني</orig>)

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Information / Wizarat Al-I'lam <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>:
- Having reviewed:
- Law No. (8) of 2016 regarding the regulation of electronic media,
- Ministerial Decision No. (100) of 2016 issuing the executive regulations for Law No. 8 of 2016 regarding the regulation of electronic media,
- Ministerial Decision No. 972 of 2022 regarding the delegation of certain competencies,
- Electronic media license No. 582/2024 issued on 25/1/2025,
- The application submitted by the licensee on 31/8/2025,
- Letter from the Director of the Electronic Publishing Department No. 60 dated 9/2/2025,
- And in accordance with the public interest.
Has decided
Article One:
By virtue of law, license No. 582/2024 for the media outlet - Al-Siyaq Al-Barlemani <orig>السياق البرلماني</orig> shall be cancelled, based on the request of the licensee, in accordance with the last paragraph, item (8) of Article (16) of Law No. (8) of 2016 regarding the regulation of electronic media, as referred to.
Article Two:
Concerned parties shall be notified of this decision, and it shall be published on the Ministry's website and in the Official Gazette.

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Information / Wizarat Al-I'lam <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Ministerial Decision No. (168) of 2025 Regarding the Regulation of Free Business Activities <orig>قرار وزاري رقم (168) لسنة 2025 بشأن تنظيم أنشطة الأعمال الحرة</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-09-14",
  "issue_number": 1756,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "decree",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>",
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains Ministerial Decision No. 168 of 2025 from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, regulating free business activities, outlining the conditions for obtaining a license, the license duration, and rules for adding multiple activities."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year 5i
of a special nature – listed in the schedule of freelance activities attached to this Resolution, which are practiced by their owners without the need for a commercial premises, as an exception to the requirements stipulated in Ministerial Resolution No. (411) of 2013 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم (411) لسنة 2013</orig> referred to.
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH – 14/9/2025 AD
</header>

Resolved

### Article One
For the purpose of applying the provisions of this Resolution, freelance activities – micro-businesses and activities of a special nature – refer to those listed in the schedule of freelance activities attached to this Resolution, which are practiced by their owners without the need for a commercial premises, as an exception to the requirements stipulated in Ministerial Resolution No. (411) of 2013 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم (411) لسنة 2013</orig> referred to.

### Article Two
Applications for issuing licenses for the companies referred to in the preceding Article shall be submitted to the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> through the One-Stop Shop Department, or through the Sahel <orig>سهل</orig> application or Sahel Business <orig>سهل بزنس</orig> application, or through any other method approved by a decision issued by the Minister of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزير التجارة والصناعة</orig>.

### Article Three
The following conditions must be met for an application to issue a license to practice the freelance activities referred to in Article One of this Resolution:
1. The entity of the company applying for the license must be a (one-person company).
2. The founder of the company must be the company's manager, a natural person of Kuwaiti nationality, fully competent, and must not have been subject to a final judgment imposing a custodial sentence for a felony or a crime against honor and trust, unless their reputation has been restored.
3. The license holder's age must not be less than 21 full calendar years, unless authorized by the court to engage in commerce.
4. The license holder must specify a chosen domicile, a post office box, or an email address registered with the Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig> according to the latest update.
5. Consent of the property owner if the chosen domicile is a private residence.
6. Submission of proof of payment of the prescribed fee.
7. Signature of the license holder on the necessary undertaking according to the form prepared for this purpose.
8. Not dealing with materials harmful to the environment, public health, or safety as specified by decisions issued by the competent authorities.
9. Any other documents specified by a decision issued by the Minister or whomever he authorizes.

### Article Four
The license shall be issued for a period of four years.

### Article Five
It is permitted to add more than one freelance activity to the same license, subject to the following conditions:
1. The added activity must be a freelance activity.
2. The added activity must be similar, complementary, necessary, or related to the granted license.
<page_end>5</page_end>

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Kuwait Today - Issue 1756 - Year 71 <orig>الكويت اليوم العدد 1756 السنة الحادية والسبعون</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-09-03",
  "issue_number": 1756,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Khalifa Abdullah Al-Ajeel <orig>خليفة عبد الله العجيل</orig>",
  "publisher": "State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page outlines several articles (Six to Fourteen) of a decree concerning freelance activities, including financial regulations, reporting requirements, and the repeal of previous resolutions, issued by the Minister of Commerce and Industry."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue No. 1756 Seventy-First Year
61
</header>
### Article Six

The license holder must disclose the commercial registration number in all official company accounts and transactions conducted by the company, while adhering to the conditions contained in the company's correspondence and summaries in accordance with Article (22) of Companies Law No. (1) of 2016.

### Article Seven

All commercial transactions conducted by the licensed company shall be exclusively through electronic payment methods.

### Article Eight

The Committee for Classification of Commercial, Professional, and Craft Activities <orig>لجنة تصنيف الأنشطة التجارية والمهنية والحرفية</orig> at the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> shall be responsible for defining the freelance activities referred to in Article One of this Decision. It may add, amend, or cancel any of these activities, and a decision to that effect shall be issued by the Minister of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزير التجارة والصناعة</orig>.

### Article Nine

Without prejudice to licenses valid at the time of issuance of this Decision, the provisions of this Decision shall apply to companies established before its issuance and those established after its issuance.

### Article Ten

The capital allocated for engaging in freelance activities licensed under this Decision shall be reduced to half of the capital required for engaging in similar activities applicable to companies. The provisions stipulated in Ministerial Decision No. (411) of 2013 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم (411) لسنة 2013</orig> referred to shall apply to matters not specifically addressed in this Decision.

### Article Eleven

The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> shall submit periodic reports to the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> on the regularity of beneficiaries of the provisions of Cabinet Decision No. (391) of 2001 <orig>قرار مجلس الوزراء رقم (391) لسنة 2001</orig> and its amending decisions.

### Article Twelve

The license holder – beneficiary of Cabinet Decision No. (391) of 2001 <orig>قرار مجلس الوزراء رقم (391) لسنة 2001</orig> and its amendments referred to – shall annually provide the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> with the following documents:
1. Bank statement for the licensed company.
2. Annual financial statements.
3. Accounts of electronic platforms and social media platforms belonging to the licensed company.
4. Any other documents specified by a decision of the Minister or whomever he authorizes.

Provided that the first fiscal year shall commence from the date of the company's registration in the Commercial Register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig> and end on the specified date for the end of the following fiscal year.

### Article Thirteen

Ministerial Decision No. (168) of 2024 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم (168) لسنة 2024م</orig> referred to shall be repealed effective from the date of issuance of the decision by the Undersecretary of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وكيل وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> specifying freelance activities. Furthermore, any provision that contradicts the provisions of this Decision shall be repealed.

### Article Fourteen

All concerned authorities – each within its jurisdiction – shall implement this Decision, which shall be effective from its date of issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Khalifa Abdullah Al-Ajeel <orig>خليفة عبد الله العجيل</orig>
Minister of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزير التجارة والصناعة</orig>

- And on Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979 regarding the supervision of trade in goods and the determination of prices for some of them, and handicrafts and the determination of prices for some of them, and its amendments.
- And on Decree-Law No. (68) of 1980 issuing the Commercial Law, and its amending laws.
- And on Decree No. (191) of 2015 regarding the organization of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (216) of 2014 issuing the Executive Regulations for Law No. (117) of 2013, which amended some provisions of Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979.

- And based on what the public interest dictates.
Has decided:
## Article One
The import of all types of poultry meat (fresh – chilled – frozen – processed) of all kinds, their derivatives and products, and table eggs, except for those heat-treated at 70 degrees Celsius, from the Kingdom of Spain <orig>مملكة اسبانيا</orig> is prohibited due to the outbreak of highly pathogenic avian influenza.
## Article Two
All competent authorities – each within its jurisdiction – shall implement this decision, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

# Administrative Decision No. (1621) of 2025
Undersecretary of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
Having reviewed:
- Decree-Law No. (43) of 1964 regarding Import and its Executive Regulations.
- And on Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979 regarding the supervision of trade in goods and the determination of prices for some of them, and handicrafts and the determination of prices for some of them, and its amendments.
- And on Decree-Law No. (68) of 1980 issuing the Commercial Law, and its amending laws.
- And on Decree No. (191) of 2015 regarding the organization of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (216) of 2014 issuing the Executive Regulations for Law No. (117) of 2013, which amended some provisions of Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (43) of 2025 regarding the delegation of some competencies to the Undersecretary of the Ministry.
- And on the letter from the Public Authority for Food and Nutrition <orig>الهيئة العامة للغذاء والتغذية</orig> No. (2085) dated 2/9/2025 AD regarding the recommendations of meeting No. (2025/8).
- And based on what the public interest dictates.
Has decided:
## Article One
The ban on the import of all types of poultry meat (fresh – chilled – frozen – processed) of all kinds, their derivatives and products, and table eggs is lifted due to the cessation of highly pathogenic avian influenza in the following areas in the United States of America <orig>الولايات المتحدة الأمريكية</orig> according to the following table:

<table_caption>US States and Counties from which Poultry Import Restrictions are Lifted</table_caption>
<table>
| State (The State) | Affected Area (The County) |
|:---|:---|
| South Dakota | Hutchinson– Aurora– |
| California | Merced– Kern– Riverside– |
| Ohio | Mercer– |
| New Jersey | Atlantic– |
</table>

## Article Two
All competent authorities – each within its jurisdiction – shall implement this decision, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

# Administrative Decision No. (1623) for the year 2025

Having reviewed:
- Decree-Law No. (43) of 1964 concerning Importation and its Executive Regulations.
- And Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979 concerning the Supervision of Trade in Goods and the Determination of Prices for Some of them, and Handicraft Works and the Determination of Prices for Some of them, and its amendments.
- And Decree-Law No. (68) of 1980 issuing the Commercial Law, and its amending laws.
- And Decree No. (191) of 2015 regarding the Organization of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (216) of 2014 issuing the Executive Regulations for Law No. (117) of 2013, which amended some provisions of Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (43) of 2025 concerning the Delegation of the Undersecretary of the Ministry <orig>وكيل الوزارة</orig> in certain competencies.
- And the letter from the Public Authority for Food and Nutrition <orig>الهيئة العامة للغذاء والتغذية</orig> No. (2085) dated 2/9/2025 AD concerning the recommendations of Meeting No. (2025/8).
- And based on what the public interest dictates.

Has decided

## Article One
The import of all types of poultry meat (fresh - chilled - frozen - processed), its derivatives and products, and table eggs, except for those heat-treated at 70 degrees Celsius, from the Republic of Argentina is prohibited due to the outbreak of highly pathogenic avian influenza.

## Article Two
All competent authorities – each within its jurisdiction – shall implement this decision, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وكيل وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
Issued on: 17 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 9 September 2025 AD

---

# Administrative Decision No. (1622) for the year 2025
Undersecretary of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وكيل وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>

Having reviewed:
- Decree-Law No. (43) of 1964 concerning Importation and its Executive Regulations.
- And Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979 concerning the Supervision of Trade in Goods and the Determination of Prices for Some of them, and Handicraft Works and the Determination of Prices for Some of them, and its amendments.
- And Decree-Law No. (68) of 1980 issuing the Commercial Law, and its amending laws.
- And Decree No. (191) of 2015 regarding the Organization of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (216) of 2014 issuing the Executive Regulations for Law No. (117) of 2013, which amended some provisions of Decree-Law No. (10) of 1979.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (43) of 2025 concerning the Delegation of the Undersecretary of the Ministry <orig>وكيل الوزارة</orig> in certain competencies.
- And the letter from the Public Authority for Food and Nutrition <orig>الهيئة العامة للغذاء والتغذية</orig> No. (2085) dated 2/9/2025 AD concerning the recommendations of Meeting No. (2025/8).
- And based on what the public interest dictates.

Has decided

## Article One
The import of all types of poultry meat (fresh - chilled - frozen - processed), its derivatives and products, and table eggs, except for those heat-treated at 70 degrees Celsius, is prohibited due to the outbreak of highly pathogenic avian influenza in the following regions of the United States of America, according to the table below:

<table_caption>Affected Regions in the United States for Poultry Import Ban</table_caption>
<table>
| Affected Region (The County) | State (The State) |
|:---|:---|
| Los Angeles | California |
</table>

## Article Two
All competent authorities – each within its jurisdiction – shall implement this decision, which shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
10 A
</header>
# Ministerial Decision No. (218) of 2025 AD regarding the dissolution of the Kuwaiti Society for National Brotherhood / Al-Jam'iya Al-Kuwaitiya Lil-Ikha' Al-Watani <orig>الجمعية الكويتية للإخاء الوطني</orig>

The Minister of Social Affairs, Family and Childhood Affairs,
- Having reviewed Law No. (24) of (1962 AD) concerning clubs and public benefit societies and its amendments.
- And Decree No. (50) of (2017 AD) concerning the Ministry of Social Affairs.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (61) of (2005 AD) regarding the Model Articles of Association for Public Benefit Societies.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (129) of 2014 AD declaring the establishment of the Kuwaiti Society for National Brotherhood / Al-Jam'iya Al-Kuwaitiya Lil-Ikha' Al-Watani <orig>الجمعية الكويتية للإخاء الوطني</orig>.
- And the approval of the Committee for the Declaration, Evaluation, and Dissolution of Public Benefit Societies and Charities, and the study and review of their Articles of Association, at its meeting No. (2025/4) held on (27/7/2025 AD).
- And the memorandum of the Assistant Undersecretary for Social Welfare and Development dated (28/7/2025 AD).
- And based on the recommendations of the Council of Ministers at its meeting No. (2025/29) - (64) of 2025 AD, held on 29/7/2025 AD.
- And after the presentation by Mr. / Undersecretary of the Ministry.
- And based on the requirements of public interest.

Has Decided

### Article (1)
The Kuwaiti Society for National Brotherhood / Al-Jam'iya Al-Kuwaitiya Lil-Ikha' Al-Watani <orig>الجمعية الكويتية للإخاء الوطني</orig> is hereby dissolved.

### Article (2)
The Board of Directors of the Society and its employees are prohibited from disposing of its funds and documents, and they must hand over what is in their custody to those assigned by the Ministry to carry out liquidation procedures.

### Article (3)
The provisions of this Decision shall be effective from the date of its issuance and publication in the Official Gazette, and the competent authorities shall be informed and implement its contents.

Dr. Amthal Hadi Haif Al-Huwaila <orig>د . أمثال هادي هايف الحويلة</orig>
Minister of Social Affairs, Family and Childhood Affairs

Issued on: 16 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 8 September 2025 AD

# Ministry of Social Affairs / Wizarat Al-Shu'un Al-Ijtima'iya <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig> Ministerial Decision No. (217) of 2025 AD regarding the dissolution of the My Mother is My Paradise Women's Society / Jam'iyat Ummi Jannati Al-Nisa'iya <orig>جمعية أمي جنتي النسائية</orig>

The Minister of Social Affairs, Family and Childhood Affairs,
- Having reviewed Law No. (24) of (1962 AD) concerning clubs and public benefit societies and its amendments.
- And Decree No. (50) of (2017 AD) concerning the Ministry of Social Affairs.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (61) of (2005 AD) regarding the Model Articles of Association for Public Benefit Societies.
- And Ministerial Decision No. (29) of 2017 AD declaring the establishment of the My Mother is My Paradise Women's Society / Jam'iyat Ummi Jannati Al-Nisa'iya <orig>جمعية أمي جنتي النسائية</orig>.
- And the approval of the Committee for the Declaration, Evaluation, and Dissolution of Public Benefit Societies and Charities, and the study and review of their Articles of Association, at its meeting No. (2025/4) held on (27/7/2025 AD).
- And the memorandum of the Assistant Undersecretary for Social Welfare and Development dated (28/7/2025 AD).
- And based on the recommendations of the Council of Ministers at its meeting No. (2025/29) - (64) of 2025 AD, held on 29/7/2025 AD.
- And after the presentation by Mr. / Undersecretary of the Ministry.
- And based on the requirements of public interest.

Has Decided

### Article (1)
The My Mother is My Paradise Women's Society / Jam'iyat Ummi Jannati Al-Nisa'iya <orig>جمعية أمي جنتي النسائية</orig> is hereby dissolved.

### Article (2)
The Board of Directors of the Society and its employees are prohibited from disposing of its funds and documents, and they must hand over what is in their custody to those assigned by the Ministry to carry out liquidation procedures.

### Article (3)
The provisions of this Decision shall be effective from the date of its issuance and publication in the Official Gazette, and the competent authorities shall be informed and implement its contents.

Dr. Amthal Hadi Haif Al-Huwaila <orig>د . أمثال هادي هايف الحويلة</orig>
Minister of Social Affairs, Family and Childhood Affairs

Issued on: 16 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 8 September 2025 AD

# Ministerial Decision No. (219) of 2025 AD

### Article (3)

- And on the approval of the Committee for the Declaration, Evaluation, and Dissolution of Public Benefit Associations / Jam'iyat Al-Naf' Al-'Am <orig>جمعيات النفع العام</orig> and Charities / Mabarraat <orig>المبرات</orig>, and the Study and Review of their Articles of Association, at its meeting No. (2025/4) held on (27/7/2025).
- And on the memorandum of the Assistant Undersecretary for Social Welfare and Development / Al-Ri'aya wal-Tanmiya Al-Ijtima'iya <orig>الرعاية والتنمية الاجتماعية</orig> dated (28/7/2025).

- And based on what the public interest / Al-Maslaha Al-'Amma <orig>المصلحة العامة</orig> dictates.
((Has Decided))

**Article (1)**
Dissolution of the Kuwaiti Strategic Planning Association / Al-Jam'iya Al-Kuwaitiya lil-Takhtit Al-Istratiji <orig>الجمعية الكويتية للتخطيط الإستراتيجي</orig>.

**Article (2)**
The Board of Directors / Majlis Idarat Al-Jam'iya <orig>مجلس إدارة الجمعية</orig> and its employees are prohibited from disposing of its funds and documents, and they must hand over what is in their custody to those assigned by the Ministry / Al-Wizarah <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out liquidation procedures.

**Article (3)**
The provisions of this resolution shall be effective from the date of its issuance and publication in the Official Gazette / Al-Jarida Al-Rasmiya <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>, and the competent authorities / Jihat Al-Ikhtisas <orig>جهات الاختصاص</orig> shall be informed and implement its contents.

## Ministerial Resolution No. (221) of 2025
### Regarding the Dissolution of the Kuwaiti Food and Nutrition Association / Al-Jam'iya Al-Kuwaitiya lil-Ghitha' wal-Taghthiya <orig>الجمعية الكويتية للغذاء والتغذية</orig>

Minister of Social Affairs and Family and Childhood Affairs / Wazir Al-Shu'un Al-Ijtima'iya wa Shu'un Al-Usra wal-Tufoola <orig>وزير الشئون الاجتماعية وشئون الأسرة والطفولة</orig>
- Having reviewed Law No. (24) of (1962) concerning Clubs and Public Benefit Associations / Jam'iyat Al-Naf' Al-'Am <orig>جمعيات النفع العام</orig> and its amendments.
- And on Decree No. (50) of (2017) regarding the Ministry of Social Affairs / Wizarat Al-Shu'un Al-Ijtima'iya <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (61) of (2005) concerning the Model Articles of Association for Public Benefit Associations / Jam'iyat Al-Naf' Al-'Am <orig>جمعيات النفع العام</orig>.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (169) of 2014 declaring the establishment of the Kuwaiti Food and Nutrition Association / Al-Jam'iya Al-Kuwaitiya lil-Ghitha' wal-Taghthiya <orig>الجمعية الكويتية للغذاء والتغذية</orig>.
- And on the approval of the Committee for the Declaration, Evaluation, and Dissolution of Public Benefit Associations / Jam'iyat Al-Naf' Al-'Am <orig>جمعيات النفع العام</orig> and Charities / Mabarraat <orig>المبرات</orig>, and the Study and Review of their Articles of Association, at its meeting No. (2025/4) held on (27/7/2025).
- And on the memorandum of the Assistant Undersecretary for Social Welfare and Development / Al-Ri'aya wal-Tanmiya Al-Ijtima'iya <orig>الرعاية والتنمية الاجتماعية</orig> dated (28/7/2025).
- And based on the recommendations of the Council of Ministers / Majlis Al-Wuzara' <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig> at its meeting No. (2025/29) - (64) of 2025, held on 29/7/2025.

- And based on what the public interest / Al-Maslaha Al-'Amma <orig>المصلحة العامة</orig> dictates.
((Has Decided))

**Article (1)**
Dissolution of the Kuwaiti Food and Nutrition Association / Al-Jam'iya Al-Kuwaitiya lil-Ghitha' wal-Taghthiya <orig>الجمعية الكويتية للغذاء والتغذية</orig>.

**Article (2)**
The Board of Directors / Majlis Idarat Al-Jam'iya <orig>مجلس إدارة الجمعية</orig> and its employees are prohibited from disposing of its funds and documents, and they must hand over what is in their custody to those assigned by the Ministry / Al-Wizarah <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out liquidation procedures.

**Article (3)**
The provisions of this resolution shall be effective from the date of its issuance and publication in the Official Gazette / Al-Jarida Al-Rasmiya <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>, and the competent authorities / Jihat Al-Ikhtisas <orig>جهات الاختصاص</orig> shall be informed and implement its contents.

- And on Decree No. (50) of (2017) regarding the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>.

- And based on the recommendations of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig> at its meeting No. (2025/29) - (64) of 2025, held on 29/7/2025.

Has decided:

### Article (1)
Dissolution of the Kuwait Project Management Association <orig>الجمعية الكويتية لإدارة المشاريع</orig>.

### Article (2)
The Association's Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة الجمعية</orig> and its employees are prohibited from disposing of its funds and documents, and they must hand over what is in their custody to those assigned by the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out liquidation procedures.

### Article (3)
The provisions of this Resolution shall be effective from the date of its issuance and publication in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>, and the competent authorities <orig>جهات الاختصاص</orig> shall be informed of and implement its contents.

Minister of Social Affairs <orig>وزير الشئون الاجتماعية</orig> and Family and Childhood Affairs <orig>شئون الأسرة والطفولة</orig>
Dr. Amthal Hadi Haif Al-Huwaila <orig>د. أمثال هادي هايف الحويلة</orig>
Issued on: 16 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 8 September 2025 AD

---

# Ministerial Resolution No. (226) of 2025
## Regarding the Dissolution of the Kuwaiti Historical Association <orig>الجمعية التاريخية الكويتية</orig>

Minister of Social Affairs <orig>وزير الشئون الاجتماعية</orig> and Family and Childhood Affairs <orig>شئون الأسرة والطفولة</orig>
- Having reviewed Law No. (24) of (1962) regarding Clubs and Public Benefit Associations <orig>جمعيات النفع العام</orig> and its amendments.
- And on Decree No. (50) of (2017) regarding the Ministry of Social Affairs <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية</orig>.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (61) of (2005) regarding the Model Articles of Association for Public Benefit Associations <orig>جمعيات النفع العام</orig>.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (11) of 2006 declaring the establishment of the Kuwaiti Historical Association <orig>الجمعية التاريخية الكويتية</orig>.
- And on the approval of the Committee for the Declaration, Evaluation, and Dissolution of Public Benefit Associations <orig>جمعيات النفع العام</orig> and Charities <orig>المبرات</orig>, and the Study and Review of their Articles of Association, at its meeting No. (2025/4) held on (27/7/2025).
- And on the memorandum of the Assistant Undersecretary for Social Welfare and Development <orig>الرعاية والتنمية الاجتماعية</orig> dated (28/7/2025).
- And based on the recommendations of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig> at its meeting No. (2025/29) - (64) of 2025, held on 29/7/2025.
- And after the presentation by Mr. / Undersecretary of the Ministry <orig>وكيل الوزارة</orig>.
- And based on what the public interest <orig>المصلحة العامة</orig> dictates.

Has decided:

### Article (1)
Dissolution of the Kuwaiti Historical Association <orig>الجمعية التاريخية الكويتية</orig>.

### Article (2)
The Association's Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة الجمعية</orig> and its employees are prohibited from disposing of its funds and documents, and they must hand over what is in their custody to those assigned by the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out liquidation procedures.

### Article (3)
The provisions of this Resolution shall be effective from the date of its issuance and publication in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>, and the competent authorities <orig>جهات الاختصاص</orig> shall be informed of and implement its contents.

Minister of Social Affairs <orig>وزير الشئون الاجتماعية</orig> and Family and Childhood Affairs <orig>شئون الأسرة والطفولة</orig>
Dr. Amthal Hadi Haif Al-Huwaila <orig>د. أمثال هادي هايف الحويلة</orig>
Issued on: 16 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 8 September 2025 AD

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756 Seventy-First Year 16
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 AD
</header>
# Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>
## Ministerial Resolution No. (15) of 2025
## Regarding the Work Schedule Regulations

The First Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of Interior, and Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>:

*   Having reviewed Law No. (28) of 1969 concerning labor in the oil business sector,
*   And Law No. (6) of 2010 concerning labor in the private sector, and its amendments,
*   And Law No. (109) of 2013 concerning the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>,
*   And Decree No. (153) of 2022 transferring supervision of the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>,
*   And Ministerial Resolution No. (302) of 2011 concerning the appointment of specialized employees to monitor the implementation of labor laws,
*   And Ministerial Resolution No. (2) of 2023 assigning the Director General of the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>,
*   And the Regulations for Rules and Procedures for Granting Work Permits issued pursuant to Resolution of the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> No. (156) of 2022 and its amending resolutions,
*   And upon the presentation of the Director General of the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>,
*   And based on the exigencies of work interest.

Has Decided

### Article One
Subject to the provisions of Law No. (6) of 2010 referred to, and in particular, Articles Nos.: (46, 65, 66, 67, 68, 82), employers shall be obligated to enter data related to daily work schedules and hours, rest periods during them, weekly rest, and official holidays, through the electronic system approved by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>. They shall also be obligated to update this data immediately upon any change thereto.

### Article Two
The data entered into the Authority's electronic system shall be an official reference for the Authority's inspectors for inspection and follow-up purposes. Upon the Authority's approval of this data, it shall be considered an official approval of the work schedule regulations, and the employer must print it and display it in a prominent place at the workplace.

### Article Three
Without prejudice to the provisions of Article No. (141) of Law No. (6) of 2010 referred to, the Authority may take legal action against employers who violate the provisions of this resolution, including partially or fully suspending the employer's file.

### Article Four
This resolution shall be published in the Official Gazette, and its provisions shall come into effect as of 1/11/2025. The competent authorities shall be informed and implement it.

First Deputy Prime Minister
Minister of Interior
Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>
**Fahad Yusuf Saud Al-Sabah <orig>فهد يوسف سعود الصباح</orig>**

<footer>
Issued on: 15 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 7 September 2025 AD

## Resolution No. (165) of 2025
Regarding a Private Marketing License for a Collective Investment Scheme Established Outside the State of Kuwait for Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig> to Market Shares of the Warba Data Center Development Fund <orig>صندوق وربة لتطوير مراكز البيانات</orig>

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, its executive regulations, and their amendments;
- And the Articles of Association and Memorandum of Incorporation of Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig>, and the agreement concluded between the representative of the collective investment scheme, Warba Advisory Limited <orig>وربة أدفايزوري ليمتد</orig>, and the marketing manager, Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig>;
- And the request from Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig> to undertake the private marketing of shares of the Warba Data Center Development Fund <orig>صندوق وربة لتطوير مراكز البيانات</orig>;
- And based on Resolution No. (04) of 2025 regarding the amendment of final approval powers for the work procedures of the Supervision Sector issued on 12/01/2025.

  "page_summary": "This page features two resolutions from the Capital Markets Authority published in Kuwait Today. Resolution No. 165 of 2025 grants a special marketing license for a collective investment scheme, while Resolution No. 166 of 2025 renews a securities activities license for Al-Khaleejia Securities Company, both signed by Ziyad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij on September 8, 2025."

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
</header>

It was decided as follows:
### Article One:
Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig> is licensed to privately market 200,000 shares (two hundred thousand shares only) of the Warba Data Centers Development Fund, established in the Cayman Islands, within the State of Kuwait. The offer price shall be 1,000 US Dollars (one thousand US Dollars only) per share, in addition to a one-time subscription fee payable upon subscription, as follows:
- 2.00% of the investor's commitment amount to the Fund.
- 1.00% of the employee's commitment amount to the Fund for Warba employees.

### Article Two:
The shares to be marketed within the State of Kuwait shall be offered exclusively to professional clients, as stipulated in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. 7 of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities and their amendments. The entity receiving subscription requests shall be:
- Warba Bank <orig>بنك وربة</orig>.

### Article Three:
The objectives of the collective investment scheme shall be determined based on what is stated in the prospectus.

### Article Four:
The marketing license duration is one year, commencing from the date of issuance of the Authority's <orig>الهيئة</orig> license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.

### Article Five:
The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this decision. In case of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, the decision shall be deemed null and void.

### Article Six:
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its respective jurisdiction. It shall be effective from its date of issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

Head of Supervision Sector
Ziad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>

# Decision No. (167) of 2025
## Regarding
A private marketing license for a collective investment scheme established outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, granted to National Investment Company / Al-Watani Lil-Istithmar <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig> for marketing shares of Leasing and Finance Fund 46 LTD

**Having reviewed:**
- Law No. (7) of 2010 concerning the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority / Hay'at Aswaq Al-Mal <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, its executive regulations, and their amendments;
- The Articles of Association and Memorandum of Incorporation of National Investment Company / Al-Watani Lil-Istithmar <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig>, and the agreement concluded between the representative of the collective investment scheme, Interfast L.P. <orig>إنترفاست إل بي</orig>, and the marketing manager, National Investment Company / Al-Watani Lil-Istithmar <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig>;

- And based on Decision No. (04) of 2025 regarding the amendment of final approval authorities for the operational procedures of the Supervision Sector, issued on 12/01/2025.

**Decided the following:**

The offer price shall be 10 US Dollars <orig>دولار أمريكي</orig> (ten US Dollars <orig>دولار أمريكي</orig> only) per share, in addition to a subscription commission of up to 2.25% of the invested amount, payable once upon subscription.

### Article Two
The shares to be marketed within the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> shall be offered exclusively to professional clients, as stipulated in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. 7 of 2010 concerning the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority / Hay'at Aswaq Al-Mal <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, and their amendments. The entities receiving subscription requests shall be:
- National Investment Company / Al-Watani Lil-Istithmar <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig>.
- National Bank of Kuwait / Bank Al-Kuwait Al-Watani <orig>بنك الكويت الوطني</orig>.

### Article Three
The objectives of the collective investment scheme shall be determined based on what is stated in the offering prospectus.

### Article Four
The marketing license shall be valid for one year, commencing from the date of issuance of the Authority's license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.

### Article Five
The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this decision. In case of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, the decision shall be deemed null and void.

### Article Six
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from its date of issuance and published in the Official Gazette / Al-Jarida Al-Rasmiya <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

# Resolution No. (169) of 2025
## Regarding the License Application Submitted by Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig> to Practice Securities Activities
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 concerning the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, its Executive Regulations, and amendments thereto;
- And the application for licensing securities activities submitted by Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig>;
- And based on Resolution No. (4) of 2025 concerning the amendment of final approval powers for the operational procedures of the Supervision Sector, issued on 12/01/2025.
Has decided the following:
### Article One:
The Authority grants preliminary approval to Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig> for licensing the activity of a custodian.
This approval is valid for a renewable period of six months, commencing on 11/09/2025 and ending on 10/03/2026, for the purpose of fulfilling the criteria specified by the Authority.
### Article Two:
The company mentioned in this Resolution shall be licensed, after completing the requirements referred to in the preliminary approval letter issued by the Authority, for a renewable period of three years from the date of issuance of the Authority's license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fee.
### Article Three:
The competent authorities shall implement this Resolution, each within its jurisdiction, and it shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.
Head of the Supervision Sector
Ziyad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>

<footer>
Issued on: 9 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 1 September 2025 AD
The Governor
Issued on: 11 September 2025 AD

## Resolution No. 189 / 1 R / 2025
Governor of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>
Having reviewed Article (21) of Law No. (32) of 1968 concerning Currency, the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>, and the Regulation of the Banking Profession, and its amendments.
And on Articles (7) and (10) of Ministerial Resolution No. 1984 regarding subjecting exchange companies to the supervision of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
And based on the request of Wall Street Exchange Company <orig>شركة وول ستريت للصرافة</orig> dated 26/8/2025 regarding the amendment of its data in the register of exchange companies at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.

It was decided
### Article One
The following amendment shall be recorded in the register of exchange companies at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig> regarding the data of Wall Street Exchange Company <orig>شركة وول ستريت للصرافة</orig>:
*   Amendment of the company's name from "Wall Street Exchange Company - Mohammed Mustafa Aba Zaid and Partner <orig>شركة وول ستريت للصرافة - محمد مصطفى أبا زيد وشريكه</orig>" to "Wall Street Exchange Company <orig>شركة وول ستريت للصرافة</orig>".

### Article Two
This resolution shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall come into force from the date of its issuance.

The Governor

# Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
Announcement
The esteemed owners of Al-Noub Al-Arabi General Trading Company <orig>النوب العربي للتجارة العامة</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation <orig>الشركة تحت التصفية</orig> have submitted
a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry to carry out / dissolve and liquidate the company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. Failure to object will result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

# Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>
Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> announces the tender for Practice No. P/MS/22/2025/2026
Supply of an automated system for managing clinics and pharmacies for Al-Sabah Specialized Medical Area <orig>منطقة الصباح الطبية التخصصية</orig>.
Specialized companies in this field, registered with the Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>, in accordance with the general and special conditions outlined in the practice documents, which can be obtained from the Ministry's website (www.moh.gov.kw) for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only.
It is necessary to attach a letter from the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> when submitting the booklet, confirming compliance with the National Labor Support Law <orig>قانون دعم العمالة الوطنية</orig> in accordance with Law No. 19 of 2000 and Cabinet Resolution No. 1104/Fifth of 2008 regarding the support and encouragement of national labor.
Please note that the closing date for the practice is at 1:00 PM on Monday, 22025/10/06, at the tenders box in the General Office of the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Sulaibikhat <orig>الصليبيخات</orig> – Ministry of Health Building – First Floor – Procurement Department – Practices Section). Bids shall be valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date, and the initial guarantee is (2%) two percent only of the bid value, valid throughout the bid validity period.
Note: Priority will be given to owners of small and medium-sized enterprises affiliated with the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني و تنمية المشروعات الصغيرة و المتوسطة</orig>.
Undersecretary of the Ministry of Health <orig>وكيل وزارة الصحة</orig>

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 AD
</header>
7

Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in that session who accepts to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be reopened in the same session based on this price.
Fifth: If the initial bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one else comes forward to bid, the auction shall be immediately reopened at his expense, based on the price at which it was previously awarded to him in the preceding session. No bid in this session shall be considered valid unless accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, execution expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and is requested for those directly involved in the sale procedures, at their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property with an inspection that negates any ignorance.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership was dispossessed is residing in the property, he shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in his favor at a fair market rent."

Vice President of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

## Announcement of a Criminal Judgment

The Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> issued, in its session held on 2021-08-19,
in Case No.: 000767 / 21 – Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> Ordinary Misdemeanors <orig>جنح عاديه</orig>
Police Station No.: (0000544 / 19 – Al-Andalus <orig>الأندلس</orig>) –
Automated Case No.: 2103063070
Against the accused: Waleed Abdullah Mohammed Al-Shayji <orig>وليد عبدالله محمد الشايجي</orig>
Nationality: Kuwait
Civil ID No.: 263122400154
An in absentia judgment ruling:
Imprisoning the accused for three years with labor and enforcement for the charge attributed to him.
The Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> hereby notifies the government of this judgment and instructs all security authorities to enforce it in accordance with the text of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedures and Trials <orig>قانون الإجراءات والمحاكمات الجزائية</orig>, noting that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the second day of publication, elapses without the convicted person appealing by objection or appeal, the judgment becomes final and enforceable against him.

Director of Criminal Enforcement Prosecution <orig>نيابة التنفيذ الجنائي</orig>

## Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>

### Corrigendum

A material error occurred during the publication of Decree-Law No. 134 of 2025 regarding the issuance of the Law Regulating the Use and Protection of the Emblems of the Red Crescent and the Red Cross, published in Issue 1755 dated 7/9/2025.
The error was found in the titles of both the Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig> and the Minister of Defense <orig>وزير الدفاع</orig>.
Therefore, we are re-publishing after correcting the error.

Property Description: (According to the attached description certificate)
Property Document No. 2012/12741 located in Abu Ftaira <orig>أبو فطيرة</orig> area – Plot No. 340 – Block No. 6 – on plan M/37883, with an area of 462.5 m2, by public auction <orig>المزاد العلني</orig> at a base price of 462,720 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> (Four hundred sixty-two thousand seven hundred twenty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the description certificate:
- The property is a private residence consisting of a basement + ground floor + first floor + second floor + and there are violations, which is additional construction on the roof.
** According to the expert's report:
On 12/6/2022, the disputed property located in Abu Ftaira <orig>أبو فطيرة</orig> area – Block 6 – Street 183 and 185 – House 1 – Plot 340 – Automated No.: 19977823, was visited and inspected on site in the presence and guidance of the defendant's agent and with the cooperation of Mr. Tariq Al-Moajel <orig>طارق المعجل</orig>, the expert of knowledge in the administration. The inspection was carried out as follows:
The door of the disputed property was opened by the defendant's agent, who stated that the defendant and her children currently reside in the property.
The disputed property conforms in terms of general and specific specifications to Document No. 2012/12741 and has an area of 462.5 m2.
The disputed property is a house located on two streets (corner) and is bordered by neighbors on both sides.
The disputed property consists of a basement, ground floor, first floor, second floor, and a quarter floor on the roof, with the following details:
a- The basement consists of: 2 stores + a large hall + a room with a bathroom + a bathroom with washbasins + a swimming pool with a shower room + ceramic floors + a sunken courtyard + a hall at the basement entrance serving as a guest dining room.
b- The ground floor consists of: 2 halls with a dining room and marble floors + 3 bathrooms + 2 washbasins + a laundry room with a small room and its bathroom inside + a room serving as an office with its bathroom + a fully equipped kitchen + the ground floor entrance is a small lobby with ceramic flooring and a skylight.
c- The first floor consists of: five master bedrooms with their bathrooms + a lobby between the rooms with wooden parquet floors + a preparatory kitchen.
d- The second floor consists of: 2 halls + 4 rooms with their bathrooms and corridor + a washbasin with its bathroom + a kitchen + a maid's room with its bathroom + a balcony.
e- The roof consists of: two rooms + a bathroom + a laundry room + a service room.
The property is externally clad with beige Sigma <orig>سيجما</orig>, beige stone, and grey marble.
The house has central air conditioning.
The house has an elevator from the basement to the roof.
There is wooden decor in various places on the ground floor and basement.
Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at the base price, and participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be reopened at his expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.

<header>
8
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 AD
</header>

- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers,
- We have issued the following Decree-Law:

# Decree-Law No. 134 of 2025
Issuing the Law Regulating the Use and Protection of
the Red Crescent and Red Cross Emblems

- And upon review of the Constitution,
- And upon the Amiri Order issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
- And upon Penal Law No. (16) of 1960, and its amending laws,
- And upon the Law of Criminal Procedures and Trials No. (17) of 1960, and its amending laws,
- And upon Law No. (4) of 1962 regarding Patents, Industrial Designs and Models, and its amending laws,
- And upon Law No. 24 of 1962 regarding Clubs and Public Benefit Associations, and its amending laws,
- And upon Law No. (24) of 1963 establishing the Supreme Defense Council, amended by Decree-Law No. (53) of 1987,
- And upon Decree-Law No. (15) of 1992 approving the Headquarters Agreement between the State of Kuwait and the International Committee of the Red Cross,
- And upon Law No. (28) of 1996 regarding the Regulation of the Pharmacy Profession and the Circulation of Medicines, amended by Law No. (30) of 2016,
- And upon the Patent Law (System) for the Gulf Cooperation Council <orig>مجلس التعاون لدول الخليج العربي</orig> States issued by Law No. (71) of 2013,
- And upon the Trademark Law (System) for the Gulf Cooperation Council <orig>مجلس التعاون لدول الخليج العربية</orig> States issued by Law No. (13) of 2015,
- And upon Law No. (75) of 2019 regarding Copyright and Related Rights, and upon Law No. (70) of 2020 regarding the Practice of Medicine and its Ancillary Professions, Patients' Rights, and Health Facilities,
- And upon the Decree issued on 12 August 1967 approving the accession of the State of Kuwait to the Geneva Conventions signed on 12 August 1949 AD, concerning the Amelioration of the Condition of the Wounded, Sick and Shipwrecked Members of Armed Forces at Sea, the Amelioration of the Condition of the Wounded and Sick Members of Armed Forces in the Field, the Treatment of Prisoners of War, and the Protection of Civilian Persons in Time of War,
- And upon the Decree issued on 3 December 1984 approving the accession of the State of Kuwait to the two Additional Protocols to the Geneva Conventions of 12 August 1949 AD, concerning the Protection of Victims of International Armed Conflicts, and the Protection of Victims of Non-International Armed Conflicts,
- And based on the submission of the Minister of Defense,

## Article One
The provisions of the attached Law regarding the regulation of the use and protection of the Red Crescent and Red Cross emblems shall be implemented.

## Article Two
The Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig> shall issue the executive regulations for the attached Law based on the submission of the Minister of Defense, within six months from the date of publication of this Decree-Law in the Official Gazette.

## Article Three
Civilian medical units belonging to the private sector, as stipulated in the attached Law, whose activities at the time of the issuance of this Decree-Law exhibit aspects inconsistent with the provisions of the attached Law, must regularize their status by removing the violating aspects within six months from the date of implementation of the provisions of this Decree-Law.

## Article Four
The Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig> and the Ministers – each within their respective jurisdiction – shall implement this Decree-Law, and it shall come into effect from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette.

Amir of Kuwait
Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>

Prime Minister
Ahmed Abdullah Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>أحمد عبد الله الأحمد الصباح</orig>

Minister of Defense
Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Salem Al-Sabah <orig>عبد الله علي عبد الله السالم الصباح</orig>

Issued at Seif Palace on: 9 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 1 September 2025 AD

# Law Regulating the Use and Protection of
# the Red Crescent and Red Cross Emblems

## Article (1)
Definitions
For the purpose of applying the provisions of this Law, the following words and phrases shall have the meanings indicated opposite each of them:
1 - The State: The State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>.
2 - The National Society: The Kuwait Red Crescent Society <orig>جمعية الهلال الأحمر الكويتي</orig>, officially authorized by the State to carry out voluntary humanitarian relief work in times of peace and war, and uses one of the internationally recognized emblems.
3 - Military Medical Units: Medical facilities that provide health services to the armed forces, their medical officers and personnel, and their affiliated means of transport.
<page_end>24</page_end>

<page_start>25</page_start>
<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Kuwait Today Official Gazette - Regulations on Red Crescent and Red Cross Emblems <orig>الكويت اليوم - أحكام شارات الهلال الأحمر والصليب الأحمر</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-09-14",

  "page_summary": "This page details regulations for the use and protection of the Red Crescent and Red Cross emblems, outlining authorized categories, specific design descriptions, and identification requirements for personnel and units, as per international conventions."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 AD
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue No. 1756, Seventy-First Year
</header>
### Article (3)
**Use of the Red Crescent Emblem for the Protection of Military Medical Units**
The Red Crescent emblem shall be used for the purpose of protecting military medical units under the supervision of the Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig> in accordance with the provisions of this Law, and the rules for the use of emblems stipulated in the Geneva Conventions of 1949 and their Additional Protocols.
Officers and personnel of military medical units must carry armbands and identity cards issued to them by the Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig>.
The Minister of Defense <orig>وزير الدفاع</orig> may authorize army officers and personnel not referred to in the preceding paragraph, and officers and personnel of the police force and the National Guard <orig>الحرس الوطني</orig>, who are trained to work when needed as nurses or assistant stretcher-bearers for the wounded or sick, to wear armbands bearing the Red Crescent emblem, provided it is a miniature approved by the Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig>. The military identity documents of each of them must prove the type of special training they received, the temporary nature of their duties, and their right to wear the armband.

### Article (4)
**Use of the Red Crescent Emblem by the National Society and State-Affiliated Civilian Medical Units**
The National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig> shall use the Red Crescent emblem for identification purposes, through its personnel, units, facilities, and transport vehicles, for the purpose of distinction, provided that the name of the National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig> is written on the emblem. The National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig> shall regulate such use as specified by the Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig>.
State-affiliated civilian medical units may use the Red Crescent emblem as part of their official emblems for identification purposes, provided this does not conflict with the provisions of this Law and the Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig>.

### Article (5)
**Use of the Emblem by Civilian Medical Units in Times of Armed Conflict**
In times of armed conflict, the National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig> may place civilian medical units at the disposal of the army. These units may be authorized to use the emblem by the Minister of Defense <orig>وزير الدفاع</orig> after notifying the National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig>, and in this case, military laws, orders, and instructions shall apply to them.
The authorization issued for the use of the emblem shall specify the conditions and rules for its use, all as determined by the Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig>.

### Article (6)
**Use of the Emblem by the International Committee and the International Federation of Red Cross and Red Crescent Societies**
The International Committee of the Red Cross <orig>اللجنة الدولية للصليب الأحمر</orig>, and the International Federation of Red Cross and Red Crescent Societies <orig>الاتحاد الدولي لجمعيات الصليب الأحمر والهلال الأحمر</orig> or any of its affiliated societies, may use the emblem in various activities they carry out in the State after obtaining a license from the competent authorities, as specified by the Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig>.

### Article (2)
**Categories Authorized to Use the Emblems**
It is prohibited – whether in peacetime or in times of international and non-international armed conflicts – to use the emblem for categories other than the following:
- 1- Military medical units.
- 2- State-affiliated civilian medical units that use the emblem as part of their official emblems without prejudice to the provisions of this Law, as regulated by the Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig>.
- 3- Private sector civilian medical units authorized to use the emblem by the competent authority. The Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig> shall specify this authority, and the conditions, rules, and controls related to this authorization.
- 4- Personnel of the National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig> and its units, and its transport vehicles, in accordance with the regulations issued by a decision of the National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig>, provided that its name is written on the Red Crescent emblem.
- 5- Anyone authorized to use the emblem in accordance with the provisions of this Law and the Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig>.

4 – **Civilian Medical Units**: The bodies, institutions, and health facilities affiliated with the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>, or the private sector authorized to provide healthcare in the State, and the transport vehicles belonging to any of them, and their medical service personnel who are practitioners of medicine and its auxiliary professions.
5 – **The Emblem**: The Red Crescent emblem and the Red Cross emblem, and their equivalents among the emblems recognized based on international agreements to which the State is a party, and for which a decision is issued by the Minister of Defense <orig>وزير الدفاع</orig>.
6 – **Red Crescent Emblem**: A drawing consisting of a red crescent on a white background, facing the viewer's right and the wearer's left, internationally recognized in accordance with the Geneva Conventions of 1949 and their Additional Protocols, as shown in the table attached to this Law.
7 – **Red Cross Emblem**: A drawing consisting of a plus sign (mathematical symbol) made of two straight lines intersecting perpendicularly, with one dividing the other into two equal halves, in red on a white background, internationally recognized in accordance with the Geneva Conventions of 1949 and their Additional Protocols, as shown in the table attached to this Law.
8 – **Armband**: An emblem placed on the left arm of the protected person, bearing the emblem.
9 – **Identity Card**: A document containing the bearer's title, full name, date of birth, personal photograph, rank, and other essential data of the bearer, prepared in accordance with the model annexed to the First Geneva Convention for the Amelioration of the Condition of the Wounded and Sick in Armed Forces in the Field, signed in 1949.
10 – **Executive Regulations**: The Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig> of this Law.
<page_end>25</page_end>

}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
10
22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH – 14 / 9 / 2025 AD
</header>
## Article (7)
### Controls and Standards for the Use of the Emblem
### and Armband and Identity Cards

The executive regulations shall specify the controls and standards for the use of the emblem and the armband, taking into account the following provisions:

1- The emblem shall be large in size and clearly visible when placed on medical units and establishments, means of transport, or to distinguish objects related to a Red Crescent or Red Cross institution during armed conflicts. The name of the using entity shall be registered on these emblems.
2- Armbands shall be used in miniature dimensions.
3- Identity cards granted by the Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig> to the categories mentioned in Article (3) of this Law shall bear the Red Crescent emblem or the Red Cross emblem.
Permission may be granted for the use of identity cards to distinguish persons associated with a Red Crescent or Red Cross institution, provided that the entities to which these persons belong are registered for these cards.

## Article (8)
### Prohibition of Using the Emblem in Association Names
### and Trademarks and Patents

It is prohibited to publicize associations, register trade names, or deposit industrial and commercial marks, industrial designs and models, and patents that use the emblem stipulated in this Law, or its name, or any name, emblem, or mark that causes confusion or similarity with any of them.

## Article (9)
### Crimes and Penalties

Without prejudice to any more severe penalty stipulated in any other law, anyone who uses the emblem or its name, whether original or counterfeit, and for whatever purpose, in circumstances other than those stipulated in this Law, shall be punished by imprisonment for a period not exceeding one year, and by a fine of not less than five hundred dinars <orig>دينار</orig> and not exceeding five thousand dinars <orig>دينار</orig>, or by one of these two penalties.
Anyone who commits any of the following acts shall be punished by imprisonment for a period not exceeding one year, and by a fine of not less than one thousand dinars <orig>دينار</orig> and not exceeding ten thousand dinars <orig>دينار</orig>, or by one of these two penalties:

1- Placing the emblem or its name on shops, stickers, advertisements, promotional leaflets, trade papers, goods, or packaging, or selling, promoting, or displaying goods bearing the emblem or its designation.
2- Intentionally damaging the emblem or rendering it unfit for use for purposes other than those for which it is intended.
3- Intentionally misusing the emblem or its designation or anything equivalent thereto, or counterfeiting it.
The penalty shall be imprisonment for a period of not less than one year and not exceeding three years, and a fine not exceeding ten thousand dinars <orig>دينار</orig>, or one of these two penalties, if the crime is committed during armed conflicts.
Without prejudice to the rights of bona fide third parties, the court shall in all cases order the removal of the violation at the expense of the offender and the confiscation or destruction of seized items or any tools used in the commission of such crimes.

## Article (10)

Without prejudice to any more severe penalty stipulated in any other law, anyone who uses or orders the use of the emblem or its name during armed conflicts treacherously to achieve military gains by leading others to believe that the scope of protection guaranteed to these emblems has been realized, and this results in severe harm to others or their physical safety, shall be punished by imprisonment for a period of not less than three years and not exceeding seven years.
If these acts result in the death of one or more persons, the penalty shall be execution or life imprisonment.

## Article (11)

The penalty shall be doubled in all cases in the event of recidivism in committing any of the crimes stipulated in this Law.

## Article (12)
### Concluding Provisions

The Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> alone shall be competent to investigate, dispose of, and prosecute the crimes stipulated in this Law.

## Article (13)

The executive regulations shall specify all controls, rules, and procedures necessary for the implementation of the provisions of this Law.
<page_end>26</page_end>

It also includes a decree (No. 176 of 2025) that amends Decree No. 391 of 2010, specifically outlining the composition and supervision of the Board of Trustees for the Kuwait Academy of Arts."
