<header>
13
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 22 Rabi' Al-Awwal 1447 AH – 14 / 9 / 2025 AD
</header>

Article (5) of the accompanying draft law permitted the National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig>, during times of armed conflict, to place civilian medical units at the disposal of the army, with a license from the Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig> for the use of the emblem for protection purposes during armed conflicts, provided that the National Society <orig>الجمعية الوطنية</orig> is notified. It also clarified the applicability of military laws, orders, and instructions to them, provided that the license for using the emblem, its conditions, and rules of use are specified in the manner to be regulated by the executive regulations of the accompanying draft law.
Article (6) of the draft law permitted the International Committee of the Red Cross <orig>اللجنة الدولية للصليب الأحمر</orig>, the International Federation of Red Cross and Red Crescent Societies <orig>الاتحاد الدولي لجمعيات الصليب الأحمر والهلال الأحمر</orig>, or any of the societies affiliated with the aforementioned Federation, to use their respective emblems in various activities they undertake in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> after obtaining a license from the competent authorities <orig>الجهات المختصة</orig> as stipulated in the executive regulations of the accompanying draft law.
Article (7) of the accompanying draft law referred to its executive regulations for specifying the controls and standards for the use of the emblem, armbands, and identity cards used by the categories mentioned in Article (3) of the accompanying draft law, taking into account the special provisions of this article regarding the size of the emblem, armband, and identity cards, in accordance with the provisions of the Geneva Conventions of 1949 <orig>اتفاقيات جنيف لعام 1949</orig> and its First Additional Protocol in this regard.
Article (8) of the draft law prohibited the establishment of societies or the registration of commercial names, and the deposit of industrial and commercial marks, industrial designs and models, and patents that use any of the emblems stipulated in this draft, or their name, or any emblem or mark that causes confusion or similarity with any of them.
Article (9) criminalized the deliberate use of the emblems or their names contrary to the accompanying draft law. It also permitted and prohibited any of them on case headings, stickers, advertisements, promotional brochures, commercial papers and goods, or packaging, or offering them for sale, selling them, or promoting goods distinguished by them. This article also prohibited their deliberate destruction or rendering them unfit for use for purposes other than their designated one, and criminalized their misuse or imitation. It mandated the removal of the violation at the expense of the violator, and permitted the confiscation or destruction of seized items or any tools used in committing any of those crimes, while respecting the rights of bona fide third parties.
Article (10) criminalized resorting to treachery <orig>الغدر</orig> in using or ordering the use of one of the emblems or marks stipulated in the accompanying draft law or its name, which involves leading the other party to believe that the scope of protection guaranteed for these emblems or marks has been achieved to gain military advantages. The penalty was intensified in case of death resulting therefrom, punishing it with the death penalty <orig>الإعدام</orig> or life imprisonment <orig>الحبس المؤبد</orig>.
Article (11) of the accompanying draft law stipulated a stricter penalty in the event of recidivism <orig>العود</orig> in committing any of the crimes stipulated therein, as it decided to double the penalty in all cases if the offender returned to the same crime or any other crime
covered by the accompanying draft law.
Article (12) restricted the jurisdiction for investigation, disposition, and prosecution of crimes contained in the accompanying draft law to the Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> exclusively.
Article (13) stipulated that the executive regulations shall specify the necessary controls, procedures, and provisions for implementing the provisions of the accompanying draft law.

### Rectification
A material error occurred during the publication of Decree No. 176 of 2025 <orig>المرسوم رقم 176 لسنة 2025</orig> concerning the amendment of some provisions of Decree No. 391 of 2010 concerning the establishment of the Kuwait Academy of Arts <orig>أكاديمية الكويت للفنون</orig>, which was published in Issue 1755 dated 2025/9/7 AD. An error was found in Article One, item (4) in the Board of Trustees.
Therefore, we are re-publishing after correcting the error.

### Decree No. 176 of 2025 <orig>مرسوم رقم 176 لسنة 2025</orig>
### Amending Some Provisions of Decree No. 391 of 2010 <orig>المرسوم رقم 391 لسنة 2010</orig>
### Concerning the Establishment of the Kuwait Academy of Arts <orig>أكاديمية الكويت للفنون</orig>
- After reviewing the Constitution <orig>الدستور</orig>,
- And on the Amiri Decree <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
- And on Law No. 15 of 1979 concerning Civil Service <orig>قانون رقم 15 لسنة 1979 في شأن الخدمة المدنية</orig>, and its amending laws,
- And on the Decree issued on 7 Jumada Al-Oula 1399 AH corresponding to 4 April 1979 AD concerning the Civil Service System <orig>نظام الخدمة المدنية</orig>, and its amending laws,
- And on Decree No. 391 of 2010 concerning the establishment of the Kuwait Academy of Arts <orig>أكاديمية الكويت للفنون</orig>, and its amending decrees,
- And based on the submission of the Minister of Higher Education and Scientific Research <orig>وزير التعليم العالي والبحث العلمي</orig>,
- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>,

We have decreed the following:
Article One
The texts of Articles (4/First Paragraph and Second Paragraph) and (6) of the aforementioned Decree No. 391 of 2010 <orig>المرسوم رقم 391 لسنة 2010</orig> shall be replaced with the following texts:
Article (4/First Paragraph and Second Paragraph):
The Academy's administration shall be supervised by a Board of Trustees chaired by the Minister of Higher Education and Scientific Research <orig>وزير التعليم العالي والبحث العلمي</orig> and comprising:
- 1- The Director General of the Academy <orig>مدير عام الأكاديمية</orig>.
- 2- The Secretary-General of the National Council for Culture, Arts and Letters <orig>الأمين العام للمجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig>.
- 3- The Deans of the Institutes <orig>عمداء المعاهد</orig>.
- 4- Two professors.
- 5- Three public figures in the field of arts.
The members of the Board of Trustees mentioned in items (4/5) shall be appointed by a decision of the Minister of Higher Education and Scientific Research <orig>وزير التعليم العالي والبحث العلمي</orig> for a renewable term of four years.
Article (6):
of the crimes

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
</header>

The appointment of the Director General and the determination of their competencies shall be issued by a decision from the Minister of Higher Education and Scientific Research <orig>وزير التعليم العالي والبحث العلمي</orig>, and their financial allocations shall be determined by a decision from the Civil Service Commission <orig>مجلس الخدمة المدنية</orig>.

Article Two
The phrase "based on the proposal of the Institute's Board" <orig>وذلك بناء على اقتراح مجلس المعهد</orig> mentioned in item 3 of Article (5) of Decree No. 391 of 2010 referred to above shall be deleted, and the phrase "one of his assistants or" <orig>أحد مساعديه أو</orig> mentioned in Article (7) of the same Decree shall also be deleted.

Article Three
Ministers – each within their jurisdiction – shall implement this Decree, and it shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Amir of Kuwait <orig>أمير الكويت</orig>
Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>

Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig>
Ahmed Abdullah Al-Ahmad Al-Sabah <orig>أحمد عبدالله الأحمد الصباح</orig>

Minister of Higher Education and Scientific Research <orig>وزير التعليم العالي والبحث العلمي</orig>
Dr. Nader Abdullah Mohammed Al-Jalal <orig>نادر عبدالله محمد الجلال</orig>

Issued at Seif Palace <orig>قصر السيف</orig> on: 9 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH
Corresponding to: 1 September 2025 AD

- And based on what was presented by Mr. / Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.

Decided
(Article One)
To close Plot No. (33A) <orig>القسيمة رقم (33A)</orig> located in South Amghara <orig>جنوب أمره</orig> area - Block (1) <orig>قطعة (1)</orig> until the violations and their consequences are removed.
(Article Two)
In the event of failure to remove the violation after (one month) from the date of closure, a more severe penalty shall be imposed.
(Article Three)
This decision shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall come into effect from the date of its issuance. The concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

Issued on: 13 August 2025 AD

## Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
### Correction
A material error occurred during the publication of Decision No. 164 of 2025 regarding the license application submitted by BlackRock Advisors UK Limited <orig>شركة بلاك روك أدفايزرز المملكة المتحدة المحدودة</orig> to engage in securities activities, which was published in Issue 1755 dated 7/9/2025 AD.
The error was in the date of issuance of the decision.
Therefore, it is republished after correcting the error.

## Decision No. (164) of 2025
### Regarding the License Application Submitted by
### BlackRock Advisors UK Limited <orig>شركة بلاك روك أدفايزرز المملكة المتحدة المحدودة</orig>
### To Engage in Securities Activities
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, its executive regulations, and their amendments;
- Law No. (116) of 2013 concerning the encouragement of direct investment in the State of Kuwait, its executive regulations, and their amendments;
- And Investment License Certificate No. 99 / 2025 issued by the Kuwait Direct Investment Promotion Authority <orig>هيئة تشجيع الاستثمار المباشر</orig>;
- And the application for a license for securities activities - foreign company branch submitted by BlackRock Advisors UK Limited <orig>شركة بلاك روك أدفايزرز المملكة المتحدة المحدودة</orig>;
- And based on Decision No. (4) of 2025 regarding the amendment of final approval powers for the operational procedures of the Supervision Sector, issued on 12/01/2025.

Decided the following:
### Article One:
The branch of BlackRock Advisors UK Limited <orig>شركة بلاك روك أدفايزرز المملكة المتحدة المحدودة</orig> is licensed, in accordance with this Article, to engage in investment advisory activities.

### Article Two:
The duration of the license for the branch of BlackRock Advisors UK Limited <orig>شركة بلاك روك أدفايزرز المملكة المتحدة المحدودة</orig> shall be three years, commencing from the date of issuance of the Authority's license certificate, and after payment of the prescribed fee.
Furthermore, the aforementioned company branch is obligated to pay the prescribed fee upon renewal of the license for any other period, in accordance with the provisions of Law No. 7 of 2010, its executive regulations, their amendments, and the decisions and instructions of the Authority.

### Article Three:
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall come into effect from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Acting Head of Supervision Sector
Fahad Abdullah Al-Fadhli <orig>فهد عبد الله الفضلي</orig>

Issued on: 3 September 2025 AD

PAHW seeks to prequalify developers from the private sector for the development of one or more of the Residential Projects in the Residential Areas described below:

All companies interested in submitting their Statement of Qualification (SOQ) for the residential project of their choice, and prior to submitting the SOQ, must pay the remaining application fees in the amount of KWD 3,000/- (Three Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) for each Statement of Qualification (SOQ), either by a certified cheque issued by an accredited bank in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> or through the K-Net <orig>كي-نت</orig> system. The Statement of Qualification / Statements of Qualification must be submitted no later than 12:00 PM (Kuwait local time) on Thursday, 30/10/2025, in accordance with the terms and requirements mentioned in the qualification document. Each Statement of Qualification (SOQ) must be submitted to the attention of the Deputy Director General for Investment and Private Sector Projects <orig>نائب المدير العام لشئون الاستثمار و مشاريع القطاع الخاص</orig> at the following address: Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> - Head Office - Investor Relations and Marketing Department <orig>إدارة علاقات المستثمرين والتسويق</orig> - Third Floor - Office No. 18 - South Surra <orig>جنوب السرة</orig> - Ministries Area <orig>منطقة الوزارات</orig> - Kuwait <orig>الكويت</orig>.

Deadline*). All interested companies should note that the RFQ will not be available for collection after the Collection Deadline. All interested companies should submit their completed Statement of Qualification (SOQ) for the Residential Project of their choice and prior to submission of the SOQ, pay the remaining RFQ Fees in the amount of KWD 3,000/- (Kuwaiti Dinars Three Thousand ONLY) per Residential Project either in the form of a certified cheque issued by a bank registered in the State of Kuwait issued in favour of PAHW or through the point of sale terminal at PAHW. The SOQ/SOQs shall be submitted no later than by 12.00 pm (Kuwait local time) on Thursday 30/October/2025 In accordance with the requirements of the RFQ, each SOQ will be submitted for the attention of the Deputy Director General For Investment and Private Sector to the following address: Public Authority for Housing Welfare, Head Quarter of PAHW, Investor Relations and Marketing Department South Surra, Ministries Area, P.O. Box 23385, Safat 13094, Kuwait.

In case of any inquiries, please send them via the official email of the Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> no later than 12:00 PM (Kuwait local time) on Thursday, 16/10/2025 (the "Clarifications Closure Date"). Responses to these inquiries will be provided via the following email: RFQ118@pahw.gov.kw. All inquiries must be submitted in accordance with the procedures and forms stipulated in the qualification document. All applicant companies are hereby notified that:
1- Any inquiries submitted after the Clarifications Closure Date will not be considered.
2- The Statement of Qualification must comply with all requirements stipulated in the qualification document.

For any clarifications on the RFQ, the Public Authority for Housing Welfare may be contacted until 12.00 PM (Kuwait local time) on Thursday 16/October/2025 (the "Clarifications Closure Date") through the following email address: RFQ118@pahw.gov.kw All clarifications must be submitted in accordance with the procedures and forms provided in the RFQ. All interested companies are hereby notified that,
1- Any clarifications or queries submitted after the Clarifications Closure Date will be not be accepted.
2-All SOQs must comply with the requirements of the RFQ

Specialized companies wishing to apply are requested to download the Declaration of Confidentiality <orig>إقرار السرية</orig> from the official website of the Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig>, which will be available for download from the date of this announcement. The Declaration of Confidentiality form must be signed and stamped by an authorized representative on behalf of the applicant company, along with a valid authorization certificate. The authorized representative of the applicant company must personally deliver a printed copy of the approved Declaration of Confidentiality form, in addition to the authorization document (in the form of a power of attorney or an official letter signed and stamped by the applicant company, stating the name of the authorized representative, their civil ID number, and a copy of their civil ID) along with their original civil ID card for verification. To receive the qualification document, a fee of KWD 3,000/- (Three Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) must be paid by a certified cheque issued by an accredited bank in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> or through the K-Net <orig>كي-نت</orig> system. The authorized representative may collect the qualification document from the office of the Manager of the Investor Relations and Marketing Department <orig>إدارة علاقات المستثمرين والتسويق</orig>, located on the third floor, office number (18) in the main building of the Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig>. The period for collecting the qualification document begins on Thursday, 18/09/2025 (during official working hours) and ends at 12:00 PM on Wednesday, 01/10/2025 (the "Final Deadline" for collection).

Interested specialized companies are requested to download the Declaration of Confidentiality from PAHW's official website available for download from the date of this announcement. The Declaration of Confidentiality must be signed and stamped by an authorized representative on behalf of the interested company along with a valid proof of authority letter. The authorized representative of the interested company carrying the copy of the Declaration of Confidentiality along with the authorizing document (in the form of a power of attorney or a signed and stamped official letter issued by the interested company identifying the authorized representative by name, civil ID number and civil ID copy) authorizing collection of the RFQ along with his/her original civil ID card for verification. Upon payment of the RFQ Receipt Fee of KWD 3,000/- (Kuwaiti Dinars Three Thousand ONLY), by certified cheque issued by a bank registered in Kuwait or K-net, the RFQ may be collected from Office of the Manager of Investor Relations and Marketing Department located on the third floor, office no. 18 at the PAHW head office. The RFQ collection period shall start on Thursday 18/September/2025 (during official working hours) and end at 12:00 pm on Wednesday 01/October/2025 (*Collection

The Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>المؤسسة العامة للرعاية السكنية</orig> reserves the right to amend the project scope or to amend, cancel, or suspend the pre-qualification application process.

## Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal <orig>ربيع الأول</orig> 1447 AH - 14 / 9 / 2025 AD

Resolution No. (55) for Meeting No. (78/2025)
The Board of Directors of the Agency decided, by majority vote of its members, to approve.
And non-approval by:
Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, Dr. Abdullah Al-Khayyat <orig>عبدالله الخياط</orig>

Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, Mr. Abdullah Dhiyab <orig>عبدالله ذياب</orig>

## Direct Investment Promotion Authority <orig>هيئة تشجيع الاستثمار المباشر</orig>
### Pre-qualification / Result

## Item 1
### Statement
*   Letter No.: D.T. 642
*   Letter Date: 2025/08/28
### Subject
*   The Authority's statement regarding the grievance of companies applying for the project to rehabilitate the permanent headquarters building of the Direct Investment Promotion Authority <orig>هيئة تشجيع الاستثمار المباشر</orig>:
*   Company meeting qualification requirements:
    *   - Al-Aam International Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة العام انترناشيونال للتجارة والمقاولات</orig>
*   Companies not meeting qualification requirements:
    *   - First Group for General Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة فيرست جروب للتجارة العامة والمقاولات</orig>
*   After listening to the entity's representative:
*   Ms. / Ebtehal Al-Misbah <orig>ابتهال المسباح</orig>, Head of Business Environment Improvement Department.
*   Decision No. (22) for Meeting No. (79/2025)
*   The Board of Directors of the Agency decided by majority of its members the following:
    *   Firstly: Approval of adding Al-Aam International Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة العام انترناشيونال للتجارة العامة والمقاولات</orig>.
    *   Secondly: Non-approval of adding First Group for General Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة فيرست جروب للتجارة العامة والمقاولات</orig>.
*   With dissent from:
    *   Member of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, Dr. –
    *   Abdullah Al-Khayat <orig>عبدالله الخياط</orig>

- This announcement is considered an invitation for interested bidders to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the bid opening session.
- Interested companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Bid Opening Department <orig>قسم فض العطاءات</orig> before the designated day for the bid opening session and bring the following documents:
1. Copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig>.
2. Copy of the signature authorization from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3. In case of attendance by a person other than the authorized signatory, a written letter of authorization from the authorized signatory, as registered with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, must be presented, delegating whomever they deem fit to attend the session.
One from the date of the announcement (copy of Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig> – personal photo – contact phone number)
Hence, this notification is issued.
Secretary General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>

# Announcement

Announces Tender No. W.Kh. 2024-2023/3 (A)
Execution of comprehensive operation, maintenance, development, and replacement works for air conditioning, electrical, plumbing, alarm, elevator, and office equipment systems at the Ministry's General Diwan <orig>ديوان عام الوزارة</orig> and its affiliated buildings.
Upon the request of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs <orig>وزارة الخارجية</orig>.
Tender documents can be obtained from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

</table>

Preliminary Meeting
(Inquiry Session)
10:00 AM on Tuesday, 10-10-2025, at the Ministry's headquarters - Arabian Gulf Street <orig>شارع الخليج العربي</orig>.
Tender documents will be published on the Agency's website for review before proceeding to purchase the documents.
- The final time for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the above announcement for bid submission.
- Bidders and practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding the submission and deposit of bids on the CD available on the Agency's website.
WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW

Regarding the issuance of Tender No. 2025/2024/26
Rental of (63) vans (4) cylinders for the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>
(Without driver – without fuel)
For a period of three years, upon the request of the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>.
Tender documents can be obtained from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

|:---|:---|:---|:---|

</table>

Preliminary Meeting
(Inquiry Session)
10:00 AM on Tuesday, 23-09-2025, at the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> building, West Mishref <orig>غرب مشرف</orig>.
Tender documents will be published on the Agency's website for review before proceeding to purchase the documents.
- The final time for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the above announcement for bid submission.
- Bidders and practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding the submission and deposit of bids on the CD available on the Agency's website.
WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW
- The aforementioned cash payment must be made by certified check or K-Net card.
- Companies/bidders wishing to submit inquiries or clarifications must adhere to submitting them to the concerned entity at the time and place specified in the table above for the preliminary meeting (inquiry session). No attention will be paid to any inquiries or clarifications submitted directly to the Agency.
- All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, except for the bid form and initial security, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- Non-divisible.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempted from the fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with Article (39) of Law No. 79/74 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law No. 2016/49.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to bid must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Care and Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
- This announcement is considered an integral part of the tender documents.
- For more information, please visit our website:
WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW
- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, must be submitted with the bid.
- The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that there is no suspension or ban on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority due to any of the violations mentioned in Article 10 of Law No. 6.

- Companies / bidders wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must adhere to submitting them to the concerned entity at the time and place specified above in the schedule for the preliminary meeting (inquiries session). No attention will be paid to any inquiries or clarifications submitted to the Agency.
- All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, with the exception of the bid form and preliminary bond, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- Indivisible.
- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, must be submitted with the bid.
- The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that the bidder's file is not suspended from government contracts registered with the Authority due to any of the violations mentioned in Article 10 of Law No. 6 of 2010 regarding work in the private sector. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the bid opening session.
- Interested companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Bid Opening Department <orig>قسم فض العطاءات</orig> before the scheduled bid opening session and bring the following documents:
1. A copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig>.
2. A copy of the signature authorization for the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3. In case of attendance by a person other than the authorized signatory, a written letter from the authorized signatory at the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> must be presented, authorizing the attendee to be present at the session.
- Owners of Small and Medium Enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempt from the prescribed fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016.
- Owners of Small and Medium Enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to bid for the tender must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development and Care <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
- This announcement is considered an integral part of the tender documents.
- For more information, please visit our website:
WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW

Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>
Correction
A material error occurred in the publication of announcements No. (0801/CA/CPC),
(CA/CMS/1083), and (CB/CMS/2073), published in Issue
1755 dated 2025/9/7
where an error appeared in the company names.
Therefore, we are re-publishing after correcting the error:
Announcement
Regarding the List of Companies Invited to Participate in
Limited Tender No. (0801/CA/CPC)

The Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries,
based on the request of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>, announces the list of companies invited
to participate in Limited Tender No. (0801/CA/CPC)
PROCUREMENT & CONSTRUCTION
CONTRACT FOR PROJECT ACTIVITIES AT
MAA REFINERY, GAS PLANT & CLEAN
FUEL UNITS
In this regard, we draw attention to the fact that, based on the text of Article (16) of
Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>, the aforementioned tender
will be offered to the following (38) companies, at least (30) days
after the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>).
A fee of (250 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) must be paid for system requests to add the company's name
to the limited tender lists. The deposit receipt for the Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> account
(KW40NBOK000000000000002036478748) must be attached with the application
submitted for this purpose to the Secretariat of the Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig>.
No single person or group of persons acting jointly may register under
more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender,
except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
However, a person who has an interest in separate companies, each independent with its own
legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus,
may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies.
The bid of any tenderer violating this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law,
in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>.
Any interested party whose name is not included in the list of companies invited to the tender
has the right to appeal their exclusion or submit a request to participate in the tender, supported by
relevant documents and addressed to Mr. / Chairman of the Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum
Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries, within (30) days from the date of this announcement.

A fee of (250) Dinars must be paid for registering companies organized to add the company's name to the limited tender lists. The deposit receipt for Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> account (KW40NBOK0000000000002036478748) must be attached with the application submitted for this purpose to the Secretariat of the Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig>.
No single person or group of persons combined may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, upon classification, register himself and each of his independent companies. The bid of a tenderer who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by judgment. This is in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>.

Regarding the list of companies invited to participate in Limited Tender No. (CA/CMS/1083)
The Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> for Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> tenders and its subsidiaries announces, based on the request of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>, the list of companies invited to participate in Limited Tender No. (CA/CMS/1083)
**Refractory (CA/CMS/1083) & Fireproofing Works in Refinery & (GP&CFU) Units at Mina Al-Ahmadi Refinery**

</header>

*   A fee of (250 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) must be paid for system requests to add the company's name to the limited tender lists. The deposit receipt for the account of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> (KW40NBOK0000000000002036478748) must be attached with the application submitted for this purpose to the Secretariat of the Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig>.

*   No single person or group of persons combined may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender. This excludes alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its own legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, upon classification, register himself and each of his independent companies. The bid of a tenderer who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law, in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>.

*   Any interested party whose name is not included in the list of companies invited to the tender has the right to appeal their exclusion or submit a request to participate in the tender, supported by relevant documents and addressed to Mr. / Chairman of the Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> for Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> tenders and its subsidiaries, within (30) days from the date of this announcement.

# Ministry of Public Works <orig>وزارة الأشغال العامة</orig>
## Announcement

The Ministry of Public Works <orig>وزارة الأشغال العامة</orig> announces the publication of Supplement No. (2) to the annual plan for supply, contracting, and service contracts to be tendered during the fiscal year (2025/2026).

### Sanitary Engineering Sector <orig>قطاع الهندسة الصحية</orig>

<table_caption>Ministry of Public Works Projects Announcement Details</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Project Subject | Detailed Objectives | Scope of Work | Type of Tender | Required Contracting Method | Number | Execution Period | Expected Announcement Date |
|:--|:---|:---|:---|:---------|:---|:-----|:---|:---|
| 1 | Study and design of the first integrated system for connecting emergency lines for all sectors and storm drains to tunnels, eliminating environmental problems resulting from the discharge of sewage into the sea during emergencies, which leads to environmental pollution and affects marine life, reducing future floods and protecting population centers and road users from the risk of floods during the rainy season. | The project aims to protect the environment and prevent the diversion of any flows to the Aoun Al-Kuwait <orig>عون الكويت</orig> area through the deep tunnel system in the State of Kuwait. | Study and design of deep tunnels in the State of Kuwait, including closing existing sewage connections with storm drains and diverting water in emergencies from pumping and purification stations to a treatment plant established for this purpose, as well as how to utilize the resulting treated water. | Method of tendering and bid submission: (Partial/Alternative Offers/Samples) - Partial not accepted - Alternative offers not accepted - Samples not required | General Practice | (A/HS/169) | 36 months | 1/1/2026 |
| 2 | Study and supervision of infrastructure improvement works for Al-Rawda, Al-Adailiya, and Al-Khalidiya <orig>الروضة والعديلية والخالدية</orig> areas. | The project aims to raise the efficiency of the sewage network, eliminate network issues due to obsolescence and end of lifespan, preserve the environment, and reduce pollution. | Study, design, and supervision of infrastructure improvement works for Al-Rawda, Al-Adailiya, and Al-Khalidiya <orig>الروضة والعديلية والخالدية</orig> areas. | Method of tendering and bid submission: (Partial/Alternative Offers/Samples) - Partial not accepted - Alternative offers not accepted - Samples not required | General Practice | (A/HS/169) | 36 months | 1/1/2026 |
| 3 | Study, design, and projects of the Sanitary Engineering Sector <orig>قطاع الهندسة الصحية</orig>. | The project aims to contract with specialized international companies in project management to coordinate with relevant project entities to overcome any administrative, financial, or technical obstacles that may hinder work progress, provide alternatives and solutions for design, supervision, execution, and project management problems, and provide technical support in preparing and reviewing time schedules for contract execution, identifying causes of delays if any, developing administrative systems for the sector to manage projects according to international and technical standards, and training national cadres. | - Conduct a feasibility study and estimated cost for the project. - Review and audit plans and designs for all works related to design and execution stages. - Provide technical support in preparing, reviewing, and following up tender documents, agreements, pre-qualification, tendering, and evaluation processes. - Project management and review of time schedules for contract execution, identifying causes of delays if any, with recommendations and solutions for engineering and technical difficulties. - Provide technical support in studying and reviewing orders and claims submitted by contractors and consultants. - Review time schedules for contract execution, identifying causes of delays if any, with recommendations, and developing administrative systems for the sector to manage projects according to international and technical standards, and training national cadres. | Method of tendering and bid submission: (Partial/Alternative Offers/Samples) - Partial not accepted - Alternative offers not accepted - Samples not required | General Tender | (A/HS/243) | 24 months | 1/1/2026 |
| 4 | Establishment of a network and treated water tanks for Phase D2 for ornamental agriculture and afforestation purposes. | The project aims to establish, operate, and maintain a network and treated water tanks for various areas of the D2 loading plan project. | - Execute works for the establishment, operation, and maintenance of a treated water network to avoid creating it with a pumping system by establishing a sub-pumping station that provides water flow within limits, and another with a natural flow system from new Al-Dakabeel <orig>الدكابيل</orig> with diameters from 300 mm to 1200 mm, with a total length of approximately 64 km, along with a control line (FOC) and all necessary civil, electrical, and control works. - Establish sub-tanks with a capacity of 0.5 million imperial gallons with their affiliated pumping stations for ornamental agriculture purposes, totaling 10 tanks in the area bounded by the extension of the Seventh Ring Road <orig>الدائري السابع</orig> to the south, up to Al-Jahra Road <orig>طريق الجهراء</orig> and the Entertainment City <orig>المدينة الترفيهية</orig> to the north, and from Al-Ghazali Road <orig>طريق الغزالي</orig> to the east to Al-Subiya Road <orig>طريق الصبية</orig> to the west. | Method of tendering and bid submission: (Partial/Alternative Offers/Samples) - Partial not accepted - Alternative offers not accepted - Samples not required | General Tender | (A/HS/201) | 60 months | 2/12/2025 |
| 5 | Study, development, establishment, completion, operation, and maintenance of the treated water system in the Southern Region of the State of Kuwait. | - Increase agricultural crops, enhance food security, and support the strategic reserve of treated water due to its positive impact on the state's economy. - Reduce imports and develop a prosperous and diversified economy to limit the state's primary reliance on oil export revenues. - Meet the demand of farm owners for treated water supply and compensate for the shortage of water reaching farms due to the increase in the number of agricultural holdings. | - Study, design, and execute the third treated water line from the Treated Water Control Center (DMC) to Al-Wafra Farms <orig>مزارع الوفرة</orig>, tanks, and their complementary works. - Study, develop, rehabilitate, execute, operate, and maintain the expansion of Al-Wafra Station <orig>محطة الوفرة</orig>. - Study, design, and execute the irrigation network and lines for Al-Wafra Farms <orig>مزارع الوفرة</orig>. - Study, design, and execute the irrigation network and cross and valley lines in the Kabd <orig>كبد</orig> area. - Study the number of agricultural options in the Al-Wafra <orig>الوفرة</orig> area and study the number of current and future agricultural connections. | Method of tendering and bid submission: (Partial/Alternative Offers/Samples) - Partial not accepted - Alternative offers not accepted - Samples not required | General Tender | (A/HS/159) | 24 months | 1/1/2026 |
| 6 | Study, development, establishment, completion, operation, and maintenance of the treated water system in the Northern Region of the State of Kuwait. | - Increase agricultural crops, enhance food security, and support the strategic reserve of treated water due to its positive impact on the state's economy. - Reduce imports and develop a prosperous and diversified economy to limit the state's primary reliance on oil export revenues, meet the water needs of farms, reuse treated wastewater, and preserve brackish water as a strategic reserve. | - Study and design the third treated water line from the Treated Water Control Center (DMC) to Al-Abdali Farms <orig>مزارع العبدلي</orig> with a length of 84 km and its complementary works. | Method of tendering and bid submission: (Partial/Alternative Offers/Samples) - Partial not accepted - Alternative offers not accepted - Samples not required | General Tender | (A/HS/246) | 60 months | 1/1/2026 |

## Announcement

The owners of Milk Silani Restaurant Management <orig>ميلك سيلاني لإدارة المطاعم</orig> have submitted a request.
## Company Under Liquidation
A request has been submitted to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry to initiate/dissolve and liquidate the company.
Legal Entity: Limited Liability Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on the objection.

A request has been submitted to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out / dissolve and liquidate the company.

Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig>, in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, towards this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, in the face of this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

## Announcement
A request has been submitted by the owners of Lon Printing Press <orig>شركة / مطبعة لون للطباعة</orig>. ## Company Under Liquidation
A request has been submitted to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to initiate / dissolve and liquidate the company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only in the face of this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on the objection.

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756 Seventy-First Year
53
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 CE

### Announcement
The owners of **Aman for Local Currency Exchange <orig>أمان لبيع وشراء العملات بالسوق المحلي</orig>** Company, currently under liquidation, have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry / Idarat Sharikat Al-Ashkhas bil-Wizarah <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص بالوزارة</orig> to proceed with the dissolution and liquidation of the company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court / Al-Mahkama Al-Kulliya <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the general partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

Legal Liquidator

# Al-Bariq Holding Company <orig>شركة البريق القابضة</orig>
## Minutes of the Adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting dated 2025/08/28

On Thursday, 2025/08/28, at 11:00 AM, the adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly of Al-Bariq Holding Company <orig>شركة البريق القابضة</orig> was held at the meeting hall of the National Shooting Company <orig>الشركة الوطنية للرماية</orig> located in - Shooting Ranges Complex <orig>مجمع ميادين الرماية</orig> - Subhan <orig>صبحان</orig> - Sixth Ring Road - opposite Jaber Al-Ahmad Military Hospital <orig>مستشفى جابر العسكري</orig>, in accordance with the invitation sent to the company's shareholders, with the attendance of:
- Mr. Saleh Adel Al-Saleh <orig>صالح عادل الصالح</orig> (Chairman of the Session).
- Shareholders owning (in person and by proxy) 233,273,120 shares out of a total capital of 45,479,200 shares, with an attendance rate of 51.292%.
After the legal quorum for the validity of the adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was announced, Mr. Saleh Adel Al-Saleh <orig>صالح عادل الصالح</orig> (Chairman of the Assembly) welcomed the attendees and then proceeded to present the items on the agenda of the Ordinary General Assembly for discussion, as follows:
Item One: Approval of the increase in the company's authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital
The increase in the company's authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital was approved from KWD 45,479,200 (forty-five million, four hundred seventy-nine thousand, two hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) to KWD 46,388,784 (forty-six million, three hundred eighty-eight thousand, seven hundred eighty-four Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) by an amount of KWD 909,584 (nine hundred nine thousand, five hundred eighty-four Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) with 9,095,840 shares (nine million, ninety-five thousand, eight hundred forty shares) at a rate of 2%, provided that KWD 40,078 is paid from the optional reserve account and KWD 869,506 from the retained earnings account, and distributed at a rate of (2) shares for every one hundred shares, equivalent to the bonus shares to be distributed to shareholders registered in the company's records until the date of the General Assembly meeting.

<header>
58
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH – 14 / 9 / 2025 AD
</header>

- Mr. Ahmed Al-Asem <orig>احمد العاصم</orig> representing Ernst & Young – Al-Aiban, Al-Osaimi & Partners <orig>ارنست ويونج – العيبان والعصيمي وشركاهم</orig>.
The proxies for the shareholders were present.
Also present was Mr. Ahmed Ali Abdulali <orig>احمد علي عبدالعلي</orig>, Secretary of the Board of Directors.
Meeting Proceedings:
Mr. Emad Jawad Boukhamseen <orig>عماد جواد بوخمسين</orig>, Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chairman of the Assembly, announced that the quorum for attendance was 100% of the shareholders holding (50,000,000) shares, in person and by proxy, out of the total capital of KWD 5,000,000 (five million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Thus, the legal quorum for the meeting was met, and accordingly, the Chairman opened the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting.
- The attendees discussed the items on the agenda, and the following was approved:
Item One: Approval of the increase in the company's authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital from KWD 5,000,000 (five million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) to KWD 15,000,000 (fifteen million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), an increase of KWD 10,000,000 (ten million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), by distributing bonus shares to shareholders registered in the company's records on the date of the General Assembly meeting, at a rate of 200% of the capital, totaling 100,000,000 shares (one hundred million shares) with a value of KWD 10,000,000 (ten million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), at a nominal value of 100 fils (one hundred fils) per share.
Item Two: Approval of the amendment to the text of Article No. 6 of the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article No. 5 of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> as follows:
Text before amendment
The company's capital was set at KWD 5,000,000 (five million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only), divided into 50,000,000 (fifty million shares), with each share valued at one hundred fils, and all shares are cash shares.
Text after amendment
The company's authorized, issued, and paid-up capital was set at KWD 15,000,000 (fifteen million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only), divided into 150,000,000 (one hundred fifty million shares), with each share valued at one hundred fils, and all shares are cash shares.
The attendees unanimously approved the amendment of Article (6) of the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article (5) of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> regarding the capital increase, in accordance with the proposed text, after obtaining the approval of the competent official authorities and endorsement in the Commercial Register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig> at the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
Accordingly, the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting of Al-Mada Hotels and Tourism Company <orig>شركة المدى للفنادق والسياحة</orig> concluded at 12:30 PM on Thursday, August 21, 2025.

Chairman of the Board of Directors

Announcement
Regarding Loss of Certificate
Based on Ministerial Resolution No. (2000/89) issued on 13/6/2000 AD regarding the issuance of a replacement certificate (for a lost one).
The Ministry of Education / Wizarat Al-Tarbiya <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> announces that Ahmed Wajih Faraj Abdullah Sayed Ahmed <orig>احمد وجيه فرج عبد الله سيد احمد</orig>, from Fahad Al-Duwairi Secondary School for Boys <orig>مدرسة فهد الدويري الثانوية للبنين</orig>, has lost his original certificate. ## Announcement
The Ministry of Health / Wizarat Al-Sihha <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Stores Department / Idarat Al-Mustawda'at Al-Tibbiyah <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Medical Supplies Control / Muraqabat Al-Lawazim Al-Tibbiyah <orig>مراقبة اللوازم الطبية</orig>) announces the following practices:

Tenders shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Stores Department / Idarat Al-Mustawda'at Al-Tibbiyah <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the Suppliers Register / Sijil Al-Mawarrideen <orig>سجل الموردين</orig>.
Companies wishing to participate in the practice must meet the following conditions:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Stores Department / Idarat Al-Mustawda'at Al-Tibbiyah <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the Suppliers Register / Sijil Al-Mawarrideen <orig>سجل الموردين</orig>.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified by an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry / Ghurfat Al-Tijara wal Sina'a <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Herbal Drugs / Idarat Al-Tasjeel wa Muraqabat Al-Adwiya Al-Tibbiyah wal Nabatiyah <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the Suppliers Register / Sijil Al-Mawarrideen <orig>سجل الموردين</orig> at the Medical Stores Department / Idarat Al-Mustawda'at Al-Tibbiyah <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> as part of the tender contents (specific to drug control).
5- Submission of samples for new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the specialized control (drugs – medical supplies).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Practice documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's / Wizarat Al-Sihha <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.
8- The booklet purchase fees can be paid through the website to be attached with the practice documents.
9- Submission of price offers in a sealed envelope, including practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's / Wizarat Al-Sihha <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.

| 3   | 5NA055      | Narcotic injections for maternal sedation, specifically for all hospitals | 75    | 6/10/2025   | 15/9/2025  |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the bid box at the Medical Stores Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Stores Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be documented with an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
<page_end>88</page_end>

4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Drug and Data Registration and Control, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department, as part of the tender contents (specific to drug control).

## Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>
### No. 2025/23, held on 24/08/2025

After reviewing the requests submitted for amending data in the birth and death records, the committee decided to publish them in the two issues listed below in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>). If the committee does not receive any objection within fifteen days from the date of publication of this announcement, the amendment will be made in the records, and birth or death certificates will be issued according to the following amendment:

## Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>
### Held on 24/08/2025, Committee 2025/23

The Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>, stipulated in Article 15 of Law No. 36/69 and formed by Ministerial Resolution No. 1650/2021, met.
*   Mr. / Director of the Central Registry Department for Births and Deaths <orig>إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد والوفيات</orig>
*   Ms. / Head of Research and Opinion Section
*   Mr. / Head of Deaths Section
*   Mr. / Head of Records Section
*   The secretarial duties of the committee were performed by Ms. / Secretary Al-Dardai <orig>الدردعي</orig>.

The committee reviewed requests from number (((296))) to number (((308))) in the attached list. After its review and verification of the completeness of documents and records, the committee decided to announce the amendments and requests in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) in two consecutive issues. If the legal period (fifteen days) from the date of the last announcement expires and no objection is submitted, the amendments will be made in the registers, and birth and death certificates will be issued.
*   Head of Births Section
*   Head of Deaths Section
*   Director of the Central Registry Department for Births <orig>إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد</orig>
*   Head of Records Section
*   Head of the General Medical Council <orig>المجلس الطبي العام</orig>
*   Committee Secretary

# Announcement of Public Auction for Car Sales
The General Department of Enforcement <orig>الإدارة العامة للتنفيذ</orig> announces that on Wednesday, 17/9/2025, and the following three days, starting from 8:00 AM, vehicles will be sold by public auction at the Public Auction Impound Garage in Al-Ardiya Al-Hirafiya <orig>العارضية الحرفية</orig>. Please note that the sale procedures will take place at the Sales Center - Al-Ardiya Al-Hirafiya <orig>العارضية الحرفية</orig>.
Note: - Payment of the full amount via K-Net <orig>الكي نت</orig> on the same day.

Please note that vehicle inspection will be at the Sulaibiya Police Station <orig>مخفر الصليبية</orig> impound on Monday and Tuesday from 8:00 AM to 1:00 PM, and the sale will take place at the Sales Center in Al-Ardiya Al-Hirafiya <orig>العارضية الحرفية</orig> at 10:00 AM.

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Kuwait Today <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-09-14",

  "page_summary": "This page contains two legal announcements for public auctions of real estate properties, detailing the sale conditions, property descriptions, expert reports, and legal procedures, published in the official gazette."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
76
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14 / 9 / 2025 AD
</header>

Against:
1- Fatima Badr Ibrahim Al-Nasrallah <orig>فاطمة بدر إبراهيم النصر الله</orig>.
2- Aseel Khalaf Muthakkar Al-Otaibi <orig>أسيل خلف مذكر العتيبي</orig>.
3- The Public Authority for Minors' Affairs <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون القصر</orig> in its capacity as guardian of the minors of the deceased (Nasrallah Badr Ibrahim Al-Nasrallah <orig>نصر الله بدر إبراهيم النصر الله</orig>, namely (Badr <orig>بدر</orig>, Raja <orig>رجا</orig>, Sheikha <orig>شيخه</orig>)).
- Property Description (according to the attached description certificate)
- Property Document No. 1169/2022 located in Al-Andalus <orig>الأندلس</orig> area – Block No. 5 – Plot 121 – Plan M 33782 – with an area of 500m². This will be by public auction with a base price of / K.D. 450,000 (Four Hundred and Fifty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the description certificate, the following violations exist:
Violations are: 1- Creation of an external door for the Diwaniya <orig>الديوانية</orig>.
2- A room made of light materials on the roof, report No. 14413.
** According to the expert's report
The expert visited the property subject of the lawsuit on 11/6/2023, located in Al-Andalus <orig>الأندلس</orig> area – Block 5 – Street 6 – Plot 121 – Automated Number (12771822), guided by and in the presence of both the third plaintiff and the agent of the first defendant, and in the presence of the knowledge expert Mr. Khalid Al-Khudair <orig>خالد الخضير</orig>.
The inspection was carried out as follows:
- The property subject of the lawsuit is an old private residence located on a single street, bordered by two neighbors, and its exterior cladding is Jordanian stone.
- The area of the property subject of the lawsuit is 500m² according to ownership document No. 2022/1179.
- The property has 3 external entrances (side entrance, main entrance, and Diwaniya <orig>الديوانية</orig> entrance).
- The third plaintiff enabled the expert to inspect the property from the inside.
- The property subject of the lawsuit consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a roof, with floor details as follows:
a- Ground Floor: Diwaniya <orig>الديوانية</orig> with a bathroom and a preparatory kitchen + (2) living rooms + maid's room with a bathroom + bathroom and washbasins + (2) master bedrooms with a bathroom and dressing room + (1) master bedroom with a bathroom + main kitchen + preparatory kitchen leading to a courtyard, the side entrance of the property, and the entrance to the first floor.
b- First Floor: Two identical apartments in terms of components, where each apartment consists of a kitchen + (1) master bedroom with a bathroom + bedroom + bathroom + living room.
c- Roof: Contains a Kirby <orig>كيربي</orig> room with a service bathroom + air conditioning area.
Property finishes are as follows:
Doors: wood + aluminum – Walls: regular paint + wallpaper – Air conditioning: split units + central.
Lighting: spotlights + pendants – Flooring: ceramic – Windows: aluminum with protection.
- The third plaintiff (Qoot <orig>قوت</orig>) stated that she, the second plaintiff (Wadha <orig>وضحى</orig>), and their children reside in the property subject of the lawsuit with the consent of the heirs, as they are divorced and have not prevented any of the heirs from entering or benefiting from the property.
- The third plaintiff stated that the first defendant (Fatima <orig>فاطمة</orig>) had been living with them until she filed a lawsuit against them two years ago. She directed the expert to the master bedroom on the ground floor, to the right of the main entrance of the property, and stated that it was the first defendant's room. The expert observed that the room was empty of furniture.
- The knowledge expert took all his observations on the disputed property and reviewed the previous expert report for the same lawsuit to assess the property's value and submit a report accordingly.

Secondly: Auction Terms and Conditions:
Firstly: The auction shall start at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Secondly: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Thirdly: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price, otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously concluded.
Fourthly: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifthly: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding will be immediately reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by the deposit of its full value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees of ownership, the expenses of enforcement procedures amounting to K.D. 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventhly: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighthly: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

Deputy Chief Judge of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year 77
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14 / 9 / 2025 AD
</header>

- The property consists of a basement, a ground floor, and a first floor.
- The basement consists of an independent hall as a storage room.
- The ground floor consists of two rooms, a kitchen, a bathroom, a maid's room, a hall, and a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig>.
- The first floor consists of a hall and 4 rooms and two bathrooms.
- The expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> inspected the property in preparation for its valuation.
(3) Session 2022/11/10: The expert's report was received, estimating the property's value at K.D. 430,000.
Secondly: Auction Terms:
First: The auction shall commence at the basic price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit, at the time of the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved fails to deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the initial bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session, and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no offer not accompanied by a full deposit of its value shall be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to K.D. 200, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in accordance with the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for it, without the Court's Registry Department <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner resides in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor accordingly."

## Description of the First Property (According to the Attached Description Certificate)

Property document no. 10084 / 2014, located in Al-Funaitees <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area – plot (145), parcel no. (8), plan M / 37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 495,000 (four hundred and ninety-five thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). (The property is a private residence (vacant land) situated on both sides of Street 815 and a main street named Al-Awad <orig>العوض</orig>, bordered by two neighbors).

## Description of the Second Property (According to the Attached Description Certificate)

Property document no. 1924 / 2023, located in Al-Funaitees <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area – plot (136), parcel no. (8), plan M / 37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 342,000 (three hundred and forty-two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). It is located on a single street, no. 815, and is bordered by vacant land on the remaining sides.

## Description of the Third Property (According to the Attached Description Certificate)

Property document no. 10084 / 2014, located in Al-Funaitees <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area – plot (138), parcel no. (8), plan M / 37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 342,000 (three hundred and forty-two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). It is located on a single street, no. 815, and is bordered by vacant land on the remaining sides.

## Description of the Fourth Property (According to the Attached Description Certificate)

Property document no. 1923 / 2023, located in Al-Funaitees <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area – plot (139), parcel no. (8), plan M / 37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 342,000 (three hundred and forty-two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). It is located on a single street, no. 815, and is bordered by a neighbor on one side and vacant land on two sides.

## Description of the Fifth Property (According to the Attached Description Certificate)

Property document no. 1931 / 2023, located in Al-Funaitees <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area – plot (140), parcel no. (8), plan M / 37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 342,000 (three hundred and forty-two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). It is located on a corner of Street no. 815 and is bordered by vacant land.

## Description of the Sixth Property (According to the Attached Description Certificate)

Property document no. 1919 / 2023, located in Al-Funaitees <orig>الفنيطيس</orig> area – plot (141), parcel no. (8), plan M / 37882 - with an area of 400 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 342,000 (three hundred and forty-two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). It is located on a corner of Street no. 815 and is bordered by vacant land.

## Secondly: Auction Terms:

Firstly: The auction shall commence at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.

Secondly: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.

Thirdly: If the bidder whose offer was approved fails to deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be reopened at their expense in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was initially awarded.

Fourthly: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with an increased bid, in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was initially awarded.

Fifthly: If the initial bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to increase the bid by one-tenth, the bidding shall immediately be reopened at their expense, based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by the deposit of its full value shall be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.

Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, the expenses of enforcement procedures amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.

Seventhly: This announcement shall be published in accordance with the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures shall do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.

Eighthly: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance thereof.

## Notice:

1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership was divested is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."
