- Property Description (according to the attached description certificate)
- Property document no. 1972/2313 located in Failaka Island <orig>جزيرة فيلكا</orig> area - Plot no. 248 - Parcel no. - from plan M/23278 - with an area of 750m2, to be sold by public auction at a base price of 300,000 K.D. (three hundred thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the description certificate:
The property is a private residence consisting of a ground floor, a roof, and annexes, according to license no. 84/28. Part of the property is demolished and dilapidated, which violates municipal regulations and systems.
** According to the expert's report:
On 16/5/2018, the expert team moved to Failaka Island <orig>جزيرة فيلكا</orig> area via the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>, in the presence of Mr. Saad Al-Daihani <orig>سعد الدعياني</orig>, the study expert, and in the presence of a surveyor from Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>, Mr. Amr Mohammed Hussein Ayoub <orig>عمرو محمد حسين أيوب</orig>. The inspection was carried out as follows:
* The property is located on three streets and bordered by a neighbor on the fourth side.
* The property is abandoned, and the buildings are demolished structures that cannot be utilized.
* The property is surrounded by a brick wall and has no doors.
* The property is approximately five hundred meters from the Failaka Island <orig>جزيرة فيلكا</orig> excavations, approximately five hundred meters from the grocery store, and approximately eighty meters from the public park.
* The surveyor from Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> recorded the dimensions and coordinates of the property's location.
Secondly: Auction Conditions:
1. Firstly: The auction starts at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
2. Secondly: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
3. Thirdly: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
4. Fourthly: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. Fifthly: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase, the bidding will immediately be reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by a full deposit of its value will be considered. The defaulting bidder will be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
5. Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
6. Seventhly: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
7. Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.

Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a full deposit. In this case, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at his expense based on this price.
Fifth: If the initial bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session, and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at his expense based on the price at which it was awarded to him in the previous session. No bid in this session shall be considered unless accompanied by a full deposit of its value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership, expenses, execution procedures amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are requested to proceed at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.

2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property has been expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent <orig>أجرة المثل</orig>."

Deputy Chief Justice of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

Announcement of the Sale of a Share in a Property by Public Auction
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction sale of the property described below, on Wednesday, 8/10/2025 AD, in Hall 5 - on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل الجديد</orig> at 9:00 AM - in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2024/180 Sales/2 <orig>بيوع/2</orig>
Filed by:
1- Ahmed Saud Abdulaziz Al-Hassan <orig>أحمد سعود عبدالعزيز الحسن</orig>.
Against: The heirs of the deceased / Ibrahim Abduljalil Ibrahim <orig>إبراهيم عبدالجليل إبراهيم</orig>, namely:
Fanouh Ali Fahad Al-Hamdan <orig>فنوح علي فهد الحمدان</orig> - in her personal capacity and as guardian of her disabled son / Ahmed Ibrahim Abduljalil Ibrahim <orig>أحمد إبراهيم عبدالجليل إبراهيم</orig>
Bashayer Ibrahim Abduljalil Ibrahim <orig>بشائر إبراهيم عبدالجليل إبراهيم</orig>.
Aseel Ibrahim Abduljalil Ibrahim <orig>أسيل إبراهيم عبدالجليل إبراهيم</orig>.
Fatima Ibrahim Abduljalil Ibrahim <orig>فاطمة إبراهيم عبدالجليل إبراهيم</orig>.
Property Description: As stated in the Municipality's property description certificate <orig>شهادة أوصاف البلدية</orig>.
An undivided share <orig>حصة مشاعاً</orig> of 50% in the property with document No. 2019/12608, located in Hadiya <orig>هدية</orig> area - Plot (9), Block No. (3), plan M/32141, with a total area of 600m², by public auction, with a base price of 165,600 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> (One hundred sixty-five thousand six hundred Kuwaiti Dinars) for the offered share.
** It was stated in the description certificate that the property is a private residence consisting of a ground floor and a first floor.
** And according to the expert's report
The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> located in Hadiya <orig>هدية</orig> area, Block 3, Plot No. 9, at the time of inspection, is as follows:
The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is a house consisting of a ground floor and a first floor, with services on the roof. It is clad in stone. There is a single-story part of the house clad in Sigma. The disputed property is bordered by two neighbors on the right and left, Street No. 1 <orig>شارع رقم 1</orig> from the front, and a main street from the back.

The expert <orig>الخبرة</orig> knocked on the door, but no one opened it. The expert inspected the disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> from the outside. The study expert <orig>خبير الدراسة</orig> reviewed the submitted documents and took notes in preparation for drafting the report.
Secondly: To ensure the conformity of the ownership documents with it, and to state the extent of what the debtor (defendants) owns in it, then to state its area, boundaries, general and specific descriptions, its possessor if any, and who has the right of usufruct if any, and its yield <orig>وربيعة</orig> if it is exploited and for what purpose.
Secondly: Auction Terms:
First: The auction shall commence at the base price indicated for the property. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, at the time of the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit one-fifth of the price.

<header>
81
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756 Seventy-First Year
</header>

Against:
1- Mubarak Shaawi Owaid Al-Mutairi <orig>مبارك شعوي عويض المطيري</orig>.
2- Dalal Shaawi Owaid Al-Mutairi <orig>دلال شعوي عويض المطيري</orig>.
3- Masha'el Shaawi Owaid Al-Mutairi <orig>مشاعل شعوي عويض المطيري</orig>.
4- Fatima Shaawi Owaid Al-Mutairi <orig>فاطمة شعوي عويض المطيري</orig>.
5- Hessa Shaawi Owaid Al-Mutairi <orig>حصة شعوي عويض المطيري</orig>.
6- Heirs of the deceased / Mariam Shaawi Owaid Al-Mutairi <orig>مريم شعوي عويض المطيري</orig>.
    a- Bader Mohammed Hamed Al-Mutairi <orig>بدر محمد حامد المطيري</orig>.
    b- Fawz Bader Mohammed Al-Mutairi <orig>فوز بدر محمد المطيري</orig>.
    c- Noor Bader Mohammed Al-Mutairi <orig>نور بدر محمد المطيري</orig>.
    d- Abdulaziz Bader Mohammed Al-Mutairi <orig>عبدالعزيز بدر محمد المطيري</orig>.
    e- Shawq Bader Mohammed Al-Mutairi <orig>شوق بدر محمد المطيري</orig>.
    f- Mohammed Bader Mohammed Al-Mutairi <orig>محمد بدر محمد المطيري</orig>.
7- Sara Faraj Fahid Al-Dhafiri <orig>سارة فراج فهيد الضفيري</orig>.

**Property Description:** (According to the attached description certificate)
The entire property of document no. 1993/4297, for which survey document no. 2024/10572 was issued, located in Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area - plot (300), block no. (2), plan M/36874, with an area of 301 m², by public auction with a base price of 270,000 K.D. (Two Hundred and Seventy Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

** According to the description certificate:**
- No violations found

** According to the expert's report:**
- The disputed property located in Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area - Block 2 - Street 1 - Avenue - House 3, automated address number 12821201. The inspection was carried out as follows:
    1- The disputed property conforms in terms of general and specific specifications and boundaries to document no. 1993/4297, with an area of 301 m².
    2- The disputed property is a private residence house overlooking two streets (corner) and Street No. (1), Avenue No. (8).
    3- The disputed property consists of a ground floor and a first floor, with the following details:
        a- Ground floor consists of 2 rooms + bathroom + hall + kitchen + external diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with bathroom.
        b- First floor consists of 5 rooms + 3 bathrooms + hall.
    4- Exterior cladding is limestone.
    5- House air conditioning consists of separate units.

**Secondly: Auction Conditions:**
Firstly: The auction shall commence at the base price indicated for the property. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of the price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Secondly: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Thirdly: If the bidder whose offer was approved fails to deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was concluded.
Fourthly: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifthly: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no offer not accompanied by the deposit of its full value shall be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventhly: This announcement shall be published in accordance with the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures shall be responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighthly: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.

**Warning:**
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> 14.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner resides in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

Vice President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

First: The auction shall commence at the base price, and participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Execution Department of the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees immediately upon the conclusion of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the initial bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session, and no one comes forward to bid with the ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at their expense, based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no offer not accompanied by the deposit of its full value shall be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transferring and registering ownership, the expenses of the execution procedures amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance.

According to the description certificate:
The property subject to the dispute is located in Jaber Al-Ali area <orig>جابر العلي</orig> – Block 4 – Street 33 – House 12, with automated number 14062376. The inspection was carried out as follows:

- The property consists of a ground floor, a first floor, a roof, and two annexes. The first annex consists of a diwaniya, a bathroom, washbasins, a storage room, and a room. Above the first annex is an apartment consisting of a hall, a room, a bathroom, and a kitchen, with an entrance from inside the property. The second annex consists of two floors, each floor having an apartment consisting of two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen.

The first floor consists of two apartments; the first apartment consists of a hall, two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen, while the second apartment consists of two rooms and a bathroom.

Notice:

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
83
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH – 14/9/2025 AD

2697 dated 19/3/2005, with an area of 1000 square meters.
. The property in dispute is a private residence (house) overlooking two streets (Damascus Street <orig>شارع دمشق</orig> and internal street No. 12), bordered on both sides. The external setback of the property in dispute, for the side overlooking street No. 12, is from the 'Seebma' (sidewalk/open space), while for the side overlooking Damascus Street <orig>شارع دمشق</orig>, it is from the 'Seebma' (sidewalk/open space) and tiles. The air conditioning of the property in dispute is central. The property also has an electric elevator and an internal staircase leading to all floors. The property has parking spaces on two sides, overlooking Damascus Street <orig>شارع دمشق</orig> and internal street No. 12. The property in dispute consists of a basement (not built on the entire plot), a ground floor, an annex, a first floor, and a quarter of a second floor, with the following details:
The basement consists of two reception areas (diwaniyas) <orig>ديوانيتين</orig>, a kitchen, a bathroom, and washbasins.
The ground floor consists of two rooms with a master bathroom, a hall, a kitchen, and another large hall. There is also a courtyard in the middle of the property, as the construction of the property in dispute is on three sides, with a swimming pool, a shower room, and a bathroom.
The annex consists of a kitchen and a room with a bathroom.
The first floor consists of three rooms with a master bathroom, a kitchen, and washbasins. There is also another room with a bathroom and a large master hall.
The second floor (quarter floor) consists of a room with a bathroom and a laundry room.
The first defendant personally stated that the current occupants of the property are the fifth defendant, Ms. Narjis Abdullah Dashti <orig>نرجس عبد الله دشتي</orig>, the second defendant, Ms. Rasha Abdul Redha Hassan Al-Shatti <orig>رشا عبد الرضا حسن الشطي</orig>, and the first defendant personally, Mr. Ahmed Abdul Redha Hassan Al-Shatti <orig>أحمد عبد الرضا حسن الشطي</orig>. He also stated that his children visit him three times a week and they have rooms in the property in dispute, and that it is not rented to others and does not generate income.
Secondly: Auction Terms:
First: The auction shall commence at the basic price indicated for the property. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a full deposit in the auction. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session, and no one immediately comes forward to bid at their expense for the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session, no offer in this session will be considered unless accompanied by a full deposit of its value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, the expenses of enforcement procedures amounting to 200 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and is requested by those directly involved in the sale procedures, at their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>
***
Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below, on Wednesday, 8/10/2025, in Hall 5 - on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل الجديد</orig> at 9:00 AM – in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2021/368 Sales/2.
Filed by: Warba Island Real Estate Company W.L.L. <orig>شركة جزيرة وربة العقارية ذ م م</orig>
Against:
Heirs of the late Abdul Redha Hassan Abdullah Al-Shatti <orig>عبد الرضا حسن عبد الله الشطي</orig>, namely:
1- Ahmed Abdul Redha Hassan Abdullah Al-Shatti <orig>أحمد عبد الرضا حسن عبد الله الشطي</orig>.
2- Rasha Abdul Redha Hassan Abdullah Al-Shatti <orig>رشا عبد الرضا حسن عبد الله الشطي</orig>.
3- Rawai Abdul Redha Hassan Abdullah Al-Shatti <orig>روای عبد الرضا حسن عبد الله الشطي</orig>.

22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14 / 9 / 2025 AD

The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, execution procedure expenses amounting to K.D. 200 <orig>200 د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and is requested by those directly involved in the sale procedures, at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges having inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been divested is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

Deputy Chief Justice of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction

The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale of the property described below by public auction on Monday, 13/10/2025, in Hall 5, 8th Floor, at the New Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل الجديد</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2024/435 Sales/1.
Filed by:
First: Abdul Razzaq Ibrahim Al-Sheikh Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>عبدالرزاق إبراهيم الشيخ صالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
Second: Ali Ibrahim Al-Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>علي إبراهيم الصالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
Against:
1- Adnan Ibrahim Al-Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>عدنان إبراهيم الصالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
2- Saleh Hamad Al-Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>صالح حمد الصالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
3- Abdullah Hamad Al-Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>عبدالله حمد الصالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
4- Adel Ibrahim Al-Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>عادل إبراهيم الصالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
5- Saleh Hamad Al-Saleh Ibrahim <orig>صالح حمد الصالح إبراهيم</orig> in his capacity as guardian <orig>قيماً</orig> over the interdicted Bader Hamad Al-Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>بدر حمد الصالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
6- Ghassan Hamad Al-Saleh Ibrahim <orig>غسان حمد الصالح إبراهيم</orig>.
7- Abdul Karim Ibrahim Al-Sheikh Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>عبدالكريم إبراهيم الشيخ صالح الإبراهيم</orig>.
8- Ibrahim Abdul Latif Saleh Al-Ibrahim <orig>إبراهيم عبداللطيف صالح الإبراهيم</orig>.

The property of document number (2021/13300) was visited under the guidance of the plaintiffs' agents, where it was found to be located in Abu Futaira <orig>أبو فطيرة</orig> suburb, Block No. (10), Street No. (96). The document refers to Plot No. (18 A + 18 B), and according to the Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig> (Kuwait Finder) program, it is Plot No. (165) with automated number (96226871). Versus: Firstly: The heirs of the deceased Ghazwa Awad Ghazi Al-Mutairi <orig>غزوة عواض غازي المطيري</orig> and the deceased Mohammed Hussein Mohsen Al-Mutairi <orig>محمد حسين محسن المطيري</orig>, who are:

## Property Description:

Street No. (98), and according to the property document, it is Plot No. (4), and according to the Public Authority for Civil Information's <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig> (Kuwait Finder <orig>كويت فايندر</orig>) program, it is Plot No. (155) and bears automated number (95521481) with an area of (24212 m2). It was found to be land overlooking the sea (from the rear facade) and overlooking the street from the front facade, with a facade length of approximately (30m). It is fenced on both facades and paved with an asphalt layer. There is no fence separating it from the adjacent land, Plot No. (296), as the separation between them is a line drawn on the paved asphalt layer at the disputed property. The disputed property contains several scattered buildings as follows:
(2) separate annexes, each consisting of a room, bathroom, and kitchen.
(1) annex consisting of an independent room (as a storage room), a kitchen, and a car garage.
An old building (old construction) consisting of a ground floor, a first floor, and a roof, with an internal staircase. The ground floor consists of (3) halls + a master bedroom + a bathroom, and the first floor consists of a master bedroom and a roof. The interior finishes include ceramic flooring, painted walls, gypsum decor ceilings, aluminum and wooden doors, and old aluminum and glass windows. There are (2) provisions for central air conditioning on the roof (without the central air conditioning unit).

As stated in the Municipality's Property Description Certificate:
Property Document No. 1992/4093 located in Al-Sabahiya <orig>الصباحية</orig> area – Plot No. 322 – Block No. 3 – from Plan No. 26061, with an area of 600m2, by public auction at a base price of (252,000 K.D.) two hundred and fifty-two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
** It was stated in the description certificate that the property is a private residence consisting of a ground floor, first floor, and roof, with no violations.
** And according to the expert's report:
The disputed property was inspected on 2023/8/21 on site, in the presence of the expert and the plaintiff on his own behalf and in his capacity, while the defendants failed to attend the inspection, as follows:
The disputed property is located in Al-Sabahiya <orig>الصباحية</orig> area, Block 3, Street 6, Plot 322, House 12, and bears the automated number: 90931342.
The disputed property is a government house consisting of a ground floor and a first floor, with annexes on the ground floor. The property has one facade facing the street, clad with limestone, and has two doors. It is bordered by a neighbor on every other side.

## Secondly: Auction Terms:
1- The auction shall start at the base price. To participate in the auction, at least one-fifth of that price must be paid by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department of the Ministry of Justice / Wizarat Al-Adl <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
2- The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
3- If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at his expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was concluded.
4- If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
5- If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the subsequent session, and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding will be immediately reopened at his expense based on the price at which it was awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by the deposit of its full value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.

Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and property registration fees, the expenses of the enforcement procedures amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventhly: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office of the Court of First Instance / Al-Mahkama Al-Kulliya <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighthly: The successful bidder acknowledges that the property has been inspected in a manner that negates ignorance.

Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Law of Civil Procedure / Qanun Al-Murafa'at <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Law of Civil Procedure / Qanun Al-Murafa'at <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Law of Civil Procedure / Qanun Al-Murafa'at <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property has been expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in his favor at a fair market rent."

Deputy Chief Justice of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
88
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 AD

*   A courtyard <orig>وحوش</orig> on the right contains an annex with an outdoor kitchen and a bathroom, and leads to another annex behind the house consisting of two rooms, a living room, a kitchen, and a bathroom.
*   The property <orig>البيت</orig> in dispute, which consists of two floors, contains the following:
    *   The ground floor contains two apartments. The first apartment consists of a living room, two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen. The second apartment has three living rooms, one room, and a bathroom.
    *   The first floor contains two apartments consisting of four rooms and a bathroom.
    *   The rooftop has only one room.
*   The property has 2 staircases leading to the first floor.
*   The air conditioning used throughout the property <orig>العين</orig> consists of individual units.

Secondly: Statement of the property owners for the purpose of dividing the property among them and clarifying the share of each one, to enable them to dispose of and benefit from their shares by utilizing, segregating, and setting them aside, provided that the property is divisible without a significant reduction in its value. In the event that it is not possible to divide it, the full value of the property will be determined by expert appraisers <orig>خبراء الدراية</orig> and the owners' shares will be specified:
The plaintiff submitted at the session on 12/7/2023 a sale contract issued by the Government of Kuwait <orig>حكومة الكويت</orig> with number 2953, dated 17/8/1992, and a certificate of interest <orig>شهادة لمن يهمه الأمر</orig> issued by the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig> of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> on 11/7/2023, through which the experts determined that the owners of the disputed property are:
- 1- Hamad Hussein Hamza Al-Mutairi <orig>حمد حسين حمزة المطيري</orig>.
- 2- Ghazwa Awad Ghazi Al-Mutairi <orig>غزوة عواض غازي المطيري</orig>.
- 3- Al-Jazi Saqr Mohsen Al-Mutairi <orig>الجازي صقر محسن المطيري</orig>.
And that the share of each owner of the property is one-third, given that they are equal co-owners <orig>ملاكاً بالسوية مشاعاً</orig>. Given that the property's area is 600 m², the property is not divisible according to the municipal regulations and systems of Kuwait <orig>اللوائح والنظم البلدية الكويت</orig>. Therefore, it was decided to seek the assistance of an expert appraiser <orig>خبير دراية</orig> from the department to determine the full value of the property, where the expert appraiser estimated the property's value at 280,000 K.D. (Two hundred and eighty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only).

Secondly: Auction Terms:
First: The auction shall commence at the basic price indicated for the property. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by the deposit of its full value shall be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the Civil Claims Law <orig>قانون المطالبات المدنية</orig> for sale procedures and at their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance <orig>معاينة نافية للجهالة</orig>.
Notice: 1- This announcement for sale by consensual auction <orig>المزايدة الرضائية</orig> is issued in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent <orig>أجرة المثل</orig>."

# Announcement of the Sale of a Share in a Property by Public Auction

Filed by:
*   Hamoud Fahad Jassim Al-Dabbous <orig>حمود فهد جاسم الدبوس</orig>.

Against:
*   1- Talal Fahad Jassim Al-Dabbous <orig>طلال فهد جاسم الدبوس</orig> in person and in his capacity as the legal representative of Al-Alamiah Goods Transport Company <orig>شركة العالمية لنقل البضائع</orig>.
*   2- Abdulaziz Mohammed Abdulaziz Al-Banwan <orig>عبدالعزيز محمد عبدالعزيز البنوان</orig> - Intervening Party <orig>خصم مدخل</orig>.

Description of the Share in the Property: (According to the attached description certificate <orig>شهادة الأوصاف</orig>)
*   An undivided share <orig>حصة مشاعاً</orig> of 50% of the property under document No. 2008/5199 located in Fahaheel <orig>الفحيحيل</orig> area - Plot (8) Block No. (33) Plan M/24516 - with a total area of 732m², by public auction at a basic price of 540,000 K.D. (Five hundred and forty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) for the share offered for sale.

# Announcement of the Public Auction Sale of Two Properties

Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14 / 9 / 2025 AD

The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction sale of the two properties described below, on Wednesday, 8 / 10 / 2025, in Hall 5, 8th Floor, New Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل الجديد</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2024/586 Sales / 2.

Filed by:
1- Maryam Nayef Abdullah Abu Rumaiya Al-Mutairi <orig>مريم نايف عبدالله أبو رمية المطيري</orig>.
2- Nashwa Nayef Abdullah Abu Rumaiya Al-Mutairi <orig>نشوى نايف عبدالله أبو رمية المطيري</orig>.

Eighteenth: Modhi Maadi Mohammed Al-Mutairi <orig>موضي معدي محمد المطيري</orig> in her capacity as one of the heirs of the late Fahad Nayef Abdullah Abu Rumaiya Al-Mutairi <orig>فهد نايف عبدالله أبو رمية المطيري</orig>.
Nineteenth: Khalid Jassim Yousef Mohammed Al-Rumaidhin <orig>خالد جاسم يوسف محمد الرميضين</orig>.
Twentieth: Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.

## Descriptions of the First Property:

1- Property document No. 1997/7533, located in Al-Ardiya <orig>العارضية</orig> area - Plot No. 88 - Block No. 2 - Plan M / 29687, with an area of 750 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of K.D. 486,000 (Four Hundred Eighty-Six Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

** The certificate of descriptions mentioned the following violations:
1- New constructions on the roof.
2- There is a structure made of light materials.
** According to the expert's report:
(1) The session began on 18 / 9 / 2022. We proceeded to the Al-Ardiya <orig>العارضية</orig> area, Block (2), Street (6), Plot (88), House (11), document number (1997/7533), which is one of the properties subject to the lawsuit. This was in the presence and under the guidance of the agent of the first appellant, Mr. Abdul Amir Aliwi Al-Shawardi <orig>عبد الأمير عليوي الشاوردي</orig>. The remaining litigants failed to attend despite being aware of the session's date. The property subject to the lawsuit is an old private residence with an area of 750 [m²] according to the document.

## Descriptions of the Second Property:

Its exterior is Sigma beige, and its area is 732 square meters, according to ownership document (sale contract) No. 5199, dated 24/3/2008.
3. The property subject to the lawsuit is an apartment building consisting of a ground floor and 11 repeated floors, according to the following details:
The ground floor consists of 11 small annexes, of which 4 annexes consist of two rooms, a living room, a bathroom, and a preparatory kitchen, and 7 annexes consist of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a preparatory kitchen.
The repeated floors (11 floors) each consist of 4 apartments, and each apartment consists of two rooms, a living room, and a kitchen.
The property in dispute has an old finishing level, where the finishes on the ground floor and corridors have ceramic flooring, unit air conditioning, ordinary suspended lighting, gypsum decorations, and plain painted walls.
5. The expert inspected one of the apartments, noting that its floors are ceramic, the air conditioning system is central, lighting is ordinary suspended, ceiling decorations are gypsum, and walls are plain painted. The building's guard stated that all apartments are identical to this apartment. The expert also inspected one of the annexes, which had begun apartment finishing except for air conditioning and units.

## Second: Auction Terms and Conditions:

First: The auction shall start at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be resumed in the same session based on the price at which the sale was initially awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full price. In this case, the bidding will be resumed in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward for Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be resumed in the same session based on this new price.

Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale of the property described below by public auction on Monday, 13/10/2025, in Hall 5, on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل الجديد</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2022/642 Sales/1.
Filed by: Fatima Abdullah Maradhi Al-Rashidi <orig>فاطمة عبدالله مرضى الرشيدي</orig>.
Against:
1- Hussein Abdullah Maradhi Al-Rashidi <orig>حسين عبدالله مرضى الرشيدي</orig>.
2- Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> for Real Estate Registration and Documentation Affairs, in his capacity.
3- Director of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig>, in his capacity.
Property Description: (According to the attached description certificate)
Property Document No. 2022/3834, located in Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area - Plot No. 327 - Block No. 5 - Plan M/36874, with an area of 301m², by public auction at a base price of 207,000 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> (Two Hundred Seven Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the description certificate:
That the property is a private residence consisting of ground floor + first floor + roof + and there are violations regarding an increase in the building percentage on the roof towards the alley and the roof bridge, report No. 14406.
** According to the expert's report:
- The disputed property located in Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area, Block (5), Street (1), Avenue (6), Plot (327), House (26), with an area of 301m², where the inspection was carried out as follows:
- The disputed property is a private residence with an area of (301) square meters according to document No. (3834). The property consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a roof. The property is located on a square meter area, overlooking one internal street and an alley. The exterior cladding of the property is made of Sigma and Jordanian stone, and the air conditioning system is "window" type. It has an entrance from the street side and an entrance from the alley side. The property is also bordered by an undeveloped plot, and there is an entrance to the property on that side and an external door which appears to be for a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig>. The fourth side of the property is bordered by an adjacent neighbor.
The property consists of a ground floor and a first floor. The committee attempted to enter the property several times, but no one opened. Upon asking the agent of the first appellant about enabling the committee to enter the property, he stated that it was not in the possession of the first appellant and he could not enable the committee to enter the property, and he merely provided guidance about it.
Upon asking the committee's expert at the department about the possibility of estimating the property's value by inspecting it from the outside only, he affirmed that he could do so. He also reviewed the previous expert report No. (Kh H 2017/2090/F) which described the property's components.
The expert took all observations and reviewed the case file to submit the report for estimating the value of the aforementioned property.
Description of the Second Property:
2- Property Document No. 1997/14238, located in Salwa <orig>سلوى</orig> area - Plot No. 597 - Block No. 10 - Plan M/33808, with an area of 500m², by public auction at a base price of 465,300 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> (Four Hundred Sixty-Five Thousand Three Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
According to the expert's report
The session began on 11/9/2022. We moved to Salwa <orig>سلوى</orig> area, Block (10), Street (9), Plots (596 and 597), Building No. (35), Document No. (1997/14238), which is one of the properties subject to the lawsuit. This was in the presence and with the guidance of the agent of the first appellant, Mr. Abdul Amir Aliwi Sharoudi <orig>عبد الأمير عليوي شارودي</orig>. The other parties failed to attend despite being aware of the session's date. Accompanied by the same expert, Mr. Abdul Rahman Al-Habib <orig>عبد الرحمن الحبيب</orig>, the inspection was carried out as follows:
The property subject to the lawsuit consists of two identical villas. The property area, according to the document, is 1000 square meters, with 500 square meters for each plot. The property overlooks two streets numbered (9 and 12) as well as an alley, and it also has a garden.
The exterior cladding of the property is stone, and it has a central air conditioning system. The property has one external entrance that extends between the two villas, separating them. There are also shaded parking spaces for cars.
The property consists of two villas, each villa comprising a basement, ground floor, first floor, and second floor, all identical. Each floor consists of two identical apartments, and each apartment consists of three rooms in addition to a domestic worker's room with a bathroom, a living room, a kitchen, and two bathrooms. Each villa also has an electric elevator in addition to stairs. The building condition of the property is moderate and in good condition. All apartments are rented.
Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall commence at the base price indicated for the property. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Once the judge approves a bid, the bidder must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose bid was approved fails to deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price, and the auction shall be resumed at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was awarded.

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1756, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 22 Rabi' al-Awwal 1447 AH - 14/9/2025 AD

one street and a transformer alley, with the exterior cladding made of stone. It is adjacent on the right side to the sewage system, and on the other side, there is an electricity transformer alley.
- The expert knocked on the door, but no one opened it.
- During the inspection, the expert found that the property subject of the dispute is adjacent to another property from the rear, separated by a wall. The expert took photographs and will attach them.
**Secondly: Auction Terms and Conditions:**
First: The auction shall commence at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved fails to deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone else comes forward in that same session who prefers to bid based on the price that
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid at one-tenth, the bidding will immediately be reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. No offer in this session will be considered unless accompanied by a full deposit of its value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in accordance with the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been divested is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

at least, otherwise the bidding shall be re-opened at his expense in the same session based on the price
at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction award may be confirmed, unless someone comes forward
in that session requesting to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a full deposit from the auction.
In this case, the bidding shall be re-opened in the same session based on the price
at which the sale was awarded.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward
with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately re-opened at his expense based on the price at which it was
awarded to him in the previous session. No bid in this session shall be considered unless accompanied
by a full deposit of its value, and the defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership,
execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees,
and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are requested
to proceed at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the
Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement,
in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose
ownership has been divested is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful
bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent <orig>أجرة المثل</orig>."

Deputy Chief Justice of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

### Announcement of Criminal Judgment

Against the Accused: Abdul Rahman Bader Abdullah Al-Enezi <orig>عبد الرحمن بدر عبد الله العنزي</orig>
Nationality: Illegally Resident <orig>بصورة غير قانونية</orig> Civil ID No.: 303100601901
An absentia judgment ruling: to fine the first accused ten dinars for the charge attributed to him.
The court ordered the referral of the civil case to the competent civil court, and the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> to set
a session for its consideration and notify the litigants thereof, and reserved the decision on its expenses.
The Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment and instructs all security authorities to enforce it
in accordance with the text of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedures and Trials <orig>قانون الإجراءات والمحاكمات الجزائية</orig>, noting that if
a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the second day of publication, elapses without the convicted
person appealing by objection or appeal, the judgment becomes final and enforceable against him.
Director of Criminal Enforcement Prosecution <orig>نيابة التنفيذ الجنائي</orig>

# Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>
## Announcement
The following is the necessary addendum to the announcement of the "Annual Plan for the Ministry of Electricity and Water <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء</orig> for the Fiscal Year (2025_2026)" published in the Official Gazette "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>" in Issue No. (1741) dated 01/06/2025.

<table_caption>Annual Plan Addendum for Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Project Name | Project Overview | Type of Offering |
|:--|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | Supply of various sound-insulated and enclosed diesel generators | The purpose of the tender is to supply diesel generators of various capacities, along with spare parts and training on operating the new generators, to cover sudden outages on the electrical grid and emergency situations. | General |
| 2 | Repair and maintenance works for various capacity diesel generators | The purpose of the tender is to carry out periodic, corrective, and preventive maintenance works for diesel generators used for emergencies in all regions of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, due to the urgent need for such works for preventive maintenance, major maintenance, and main maintenance of diesel-powered electricity generators. | General |
</table>

And those specialized companies wishing to participate in this practice must obtain the practice documents for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only, from the Financial Affairs Department - Contracts Section - Second Floor - National Council for Culture, Arts and Letters <orig>المجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig> Building - Al-Shuhada Street <orig>شارع الشهداء</orig> - Sharq <orig>الشرق</orig>.
Subject to adherence to the following:
1- The practice is indivisible, and alternative offers will not be accepted.
2- The deadline for submitting bids is within (10 working days) from the date of publication of the announcement in Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> newspaper.
3- All documents must be submitted on (CD) in 3 copies, with the exception of (the bid form, preliminary insurance, a copy of the purchase receipt, and the practitioner's data form).
4- A preliminary meeting will be held (5 working days) after the date of publication of the announcement to answer practitioners' inquiries, at Al-Qibliya School <orig>المدرسة القبلية</orig> Building, Meeting Room, Ground Floor, at 10:00 AM, in accordance with Article (7) of the General Conditions of Practice.
5- This announcement serves as an invitation for practitioners wishing to attend the bid opening session, after coordination with the Procurement Control (Contracts Section) before the scheduled date for the bid opening session.

Secretary General <orig>الأمين العام</orig>

Note: (The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> may cancel the practice without stating reasons and without any objection from the practitioner).

The Authority did not provide any evidence of legal action taken from the date the debt became due until the date of the bankruptcy declaration judgment, and therefore its right has lapsed by prescription according to the text of Article (118) of the Kuwaiti Commercial Law <orig>قانون التجارة الكويتي</orig>. |
| 3 | United Contracting Company <orig>الشركة المشتركة للمقاولات</orig> | 66,629.995 K.D. | As per the financial position report prepared by the Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig>, and it did not submit a request to list its debt to the trustee in his capacity according to the text of Article (105) of Law No. (2020/71). |
| 4 | United Contracting Company <orig>الشركة المشتركة للم
<page_end>112</page_end>

# Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي</orig>
## Announcement
The Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig> announces the publication of the announcement for Practice No.: PAAET / SAM / 26-2025/2026, concerning the supply, installation, and warranty of directional signs outside the buildings of the Authority's colleges and institutes, according to the terms and specifications stated in the practice documents.
Companies and institutions wishing to participate in this practice should visit the Public Authority for Applied Education and Training <orig>الهيئة العامة للتعليم التطبيقي والتدريب</orig> website (www.paaet.edu.kw) to purchase the practice tender listed under electronic services (general services) and submit bids to the Authority's General Office located in Shuwaikh Educational Area <orig>منطقة الشويخ التعليمية</orig> – Supplies Department <orig>إدارة التوريدات</orig> within one week from this date, against a non-refundable fee of (K.D. 75.000).
The Director General <orig>المدير العام</orig>

# Public Authority for Sports <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig>
## Announcement
The Public Authority for Sports <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> announces the re-issuance of Practice No. PASD 2026/2025/16 concerning electrical maintenance works and replacement of lighting fixtures for squash courts at the Kuwait Squash Federation <orig>الاتحاد الكويتي للاسكواش</orig>, in sealed envelopes according to the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents, which can be obtained from the Services and Supplies Department <orig>إدارة الخدمات والتوريدات</orig> – Tenders and Practices Section <orig>قسم المناقصات والممارسات</orig> – Ground Floor, Office No. (5) at the Authority's headquarters in Al-Riqqa Area <orig>منطقة الرقعي</orig> during official working hours or through the Public Authority for Sports <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).

<table_caption>Tender Details for the Public Authority for Sports</table_caption>
<table>
| Issue Date | Closing Date | Document Price | Initial Guarantee |
|---|---|---|---|
| 14/9/2025 | 29/9/2025 | K.D. 75 | (K.D. 1500) One Thousand Five Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars only, in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee |
</table>

<table_caption>Tender Schedule for the Public Authority for Sports</table_caption>
<table>
| Preliminary Meeting (Inquiry Session) (First) | Validity for (90) days in favor of the Public Authority for Sports <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> from the closing date |
|---|---|
| 11:00 AM on Sunday, 21/9/2025 AD, at the Public Authority for Sports <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> | |
</table>

Bids must be submitted from 9:00 AM until 2:00 PM on the closing date. Bids must be delivered in sealed envelopes with red wax and placed in the box designated for practices at the Authority's headquarters (Second Floor). No bids received after the specified closing time for the practice will be accepted.
- Practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding submitting bids (CD) on the Public Authority for Sports <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).
- Companies/practitioners wishing to submit inquiries or clarifications must do so at the time and place specified above in the Preliminary Meeting (Inquiry Session) schedule. No inquiries will be considered after the deadline.
- All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-copyable hard copy, except for the bid form and initial insurance, which must be submitted as a hard copy.
Bids shall be valid for (90) ninety days from the date of opening bids. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for purchasing the practice documents, the initial guarantee, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
- The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority or any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
- The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating clearance from consumption debts.
The practice is open to all companies and institutions specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sports <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, against a non-refundable fee of (K.D. 75) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> circulars), bringing with them the following: -
1- A copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.
2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
3- A written letter of authorized delegation with the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig> – a copy of the signature authorization).
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempted from the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. (49/2016).
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to apply for the practice must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development and Care <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, including their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
In accordance with the text of Article (48) of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. (49/2016), which states: "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the practice documents in a public session in the presence of bidders or their representatives."
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the bid opening session by coordinating with the competent committee before the session date.

# Announcement

Regarding the re-tender of Practice No. 4 - 2025 concerning the installation, operation, and maintenance of mechanical equipment, fire-fighting networks, and small steel structures belonging to the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>.
The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces the re-tender of Practice No. 4 - 2025 concerning the installation, operation, and maintenance of mechanical equipment, fire-fighting networks, and small steel structures belonging to the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>.
These documents can be obtained by visiting the website bids.pai.gov.kw starting from the date of publication of this announcement.

<table_caption>Tender Details for Practice No. 4-2025</table_caption>
<table>
| Tender | Closing Date | Document Price | Initial Deposit | Preliminary Meeting |
|:------|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 14/9/2025 | 23/10/2025 | K.D. 75 | 1500 | Day: Monday <br> Date: 22/9/2025 <br> Location: Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> – South Surra – Ground Floor, Main Meeting Room. Time: 10:00 AM |
</table>

The deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 23/10/2025, until 12:00 PM. Bids shall be submitted at the main headquarters of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> (Second Floor – Supplies and Stores Department – Procurement Section) in an envelope marked with the practice name. Bids shall be valid for (90) days from the date of opening the bid envelopes.
The practitioner must submit a recent 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the company's file regarding government contracts registered with the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, and a 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate confirming compliance with the national labor percentage, dated contemporaneously with the bid date. The practitioner must also deposit with their bid an initial deposit in the form of a certified check or an unconditional, irrevocable, and reservation-free letter of guarantee issued in the name of the bidder by one of the accredited banks in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> and in favor of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>, valid for the duration of the bid. Any bid not accompanied by the full amount of this deposit will be excluded. The initial deposit may not be refunded until (90) days have passed from the closing date of the practice or when the winning practitioner signs the contract, unless the practice is cancelled. The Authority will not pay any interest on the amount of this deposit, and the practitioner's creditors may not seize its amount, noting that this practice is indivisible.

The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces, based on the decision of the Authority's Board of Directors at its meeting No. (2025/5) held on August 27, 2025, which included the cancellation of a number of industrial licenses and the withdrawal of their associated industrial plots, as well as the withdrawal of service plots and the cancellation of their associated contracts as listed in the attached schedules, that it is no longer responsible for any changes affecting these plots from the date of the Board of Directors' decision. Beneficiaries of these plots must hand them over to the Authority free of encumbrances within ten days from the date of this announcement, otherwise the Authority will be compelled to take legal action against them.

# Announcement
The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces that Mr. Abdullatif Khalid Abdullatif Al-Otaiqi <orig>عبداللطيف خالد عبداللطيف العتيقي</orig> has applied for a replacement for a lost plot contract No. (143), plot No. (1) (Shuwaikh Industrial-3 <orig>الشويخ الصناعية-3</orig>). # Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig>
## Announcement of Practice H.M.M. 6 - 2025/2026
Regarding the purchase of HHD Shredder machines and equipment
The Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig> announces a sealed envelope practice for the purchase of HHD Shredder machines and equipment, as detailed in the booklet:
1.  These documents can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department – Treasury Section (South Surra – Ministries Area – Ground Floor) during official working hours for a fee not exceeding K.D. 50/- (Fifty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only).
2.  The latest deadline for submitting bids to the Financial Affairs Department is 12:00 PM on Thursday, 25/9/2025. Any bid submitted after this time will be rejected.
3.  The amount of the initial guarantee must not be less than 2% (two percent) of the practice bid value, and the guarantee must be issued by one of the approved local banks in Arabic and remain valid throughout the bid validity period.
4.  The final guarantee amount is 10% (ten percent) of the total contract value, provided that this guarantee is issued by one of the approved local banks in Arabic.
5.  The bid shall remain valid for 90 days (ninety days) from the date of opening the bid envelopes.
6.  Alternative offers are not accepted.
7.  The practice is indivisible.

# Announcement
The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces the decision of the Allocation Committee <orig>لجنة التخصيص</orig> taken at its meeting No. (2025/7) held on 24/8/2025, regarding the approval of the withdrawal of the following 'Drakil' (sand quarries) due to their violation of Ministerial Resolution No. (2018/4) concerning the rules and regulations for temporary allocation of sand quarry sites (Drakil Al-Rimal <orig>دراكيـل الرمال</orig>):

| 2 | Al-Mabrouk Trading and Contracting Establishment (2) <orig>مؤسسة المبروك للتجارة والمقاولات</orig> | Jahra Drakil Area <orig>منطقة دراكيل الجهراء</orig> Drakil (2) |

Otherwise, the Authority will be compelled to take administrative measures for removal.

# General Directorate of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>
Announcement
Practice No. (22 - 2025/2026)
Licenses for Engineering Drawing Software and Other Miscellaneous Items
The General Directorate of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig> announces the offering of Practice No. (22-2025/2026) related to licenses for engineering drawing software and other miscellaneous items at the General Directorate of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>, in accordance with the terms and specifications mentioned in the practice documents, with adherence to making appointments for government entities as per the esteemed Council of Ministers' decisions. These documents can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department - Tenders and Contracts Section at the General Directorate of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig> starting from Sunday, 2025/09/14, during official working hours, upon payment of an amount of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only, provided that payment is made via K.net.
A preliminary meeting will be held at the headquarters of the General Directorate of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig> on Tuesday, 2025/09/23, at 11:00 AM.
The documents shall be returned after being filled out, with the required documents attached, and an initial security deposit of no less than (2%) of the bid value, in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee issued by one of the accredited banks in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, issued in the name of the bidder and in favor of the General Directorate of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>, and without any restriction or condition. Bids not accompanied by this security deposit will not be considered, even if they conform to the specifications. The security deposit must be valid for the duration of the required bid validity, and the documents shall be submitted in an official envelope sealed with red wax. Bids will be submitted to the (Tenders and Contracts Section) at the General Directorate of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>.
Please note that the deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Wednesday, 2025/10/01, and any bid submitted after this deadline will be rejected.
Acting Deputy Director General for Administrative and Financial Affairs

5.  The bid shall remain valid for 90 days (ninety days) from the date of opening the bid envelopes.
