along with providing proof thereof.
3. The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> will begin issuing the practice terms starting from the date of publication of this announcement and for a period of 10 days.
4. The practice terms can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only.
5. The preliminary meeting with the bidders will be held on Sunday, 21/09/2025, at 11:00 AM in the building of the General Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Planning <orig>الأمانة العامة للمجلس الأعلى للتخطيط</orig> – Second Floor – Jibla Hall <orig>قاعة جبلة</orig>.
6. Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Financial Affairs Department at the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> no later than 1:00 PM on Thursday, 25/09/2025.

### Announcement
The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> announces its desire to issue Practice No. (2026/2025-2) for the renewal of licenses for horses <orig>الخيل</orig> coming from firewalls for the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>. Specialized companies wishing to apply for this practice must observe the following:
1. The company must be registered with the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>.
2. The applying company must have experience in this field prior to the issuance of this announcement, along with providing proof thereof.
3. The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> will begin issuing the practice terms starting from the date of publication of this announcement and for a period of 10 days.
4. The practice terms can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only.
5. The preliminary meeting with the bidders will be held on Sunday, 21/09/2025, at 11:00 AM in the building of the General Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Planning <orig>الأمانة العامة للمجلس الأعلى للتخطيط</orig> – Second Floor – Jibla Hall <orig>قاعة جبلة</orig>.
6. Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Financial Affairs Department at the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> no later than 1:00 PM on Thursday, 25/09/2025.

### Announcement
The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> announces its desire to issue Practice No. (2026/2025-9) for the renewal of licenses, maintenance of network protection devices, and work distribution. Specialized companies wishing to apply for this practice must observe the following:
1. The company must be registered with the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>.
2. The applying company must have experience in this field prior to the issuance of this announcement, along with providing proof thereof.
3. The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> will begin issuing the practice terms starting from the date of publication of this announcement and for a period of 10 days.
4. The practice terms can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only.
5. The preliminary meeting with the bidders will be held on Sunday, 21/09/2025, at 11:00 AM in the building of the General Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Planning <orig>الأمانة العامة للمجلس الأعلى للتخطيط</orig> – Second Floor – Jibla Hall <orig>قاعة جبلة</orig>.
6. Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Financial Affairs Department at the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> no later than 1:00 PM on Thursday, 25/09/2025.

## Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig>
### Bid Opening

- **No.**: 1
  - **Statement**: Ref. No.: H.H.R / 8 / 2024 / 2025
    Decision No. (1) for Meeting No. (2025/77)
  - **Subject**: Tender for the purchase, supply, and maintenance of an X-ray device for the Radiology Department at the Sports Heart Center.
    The bids submitted for the tender, numbering (7), were opened according to the price list.
    The Board of Directors of the Authority decided:
    First: To exclude the following companies:
    - Warba Medical Equipment Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة وربة للتجهيزات الطبية ذ م م</orig>
    This is based on the provisions of Article (45) of Public Tenders Law No. (49) of 2016, due to the failure to submit a bank guarantee that does not mention the subject of the tender.
    Second: To refer the submitted tender documents to the concerned entity for study and to provide the necessary recommendations within (30) days from this date.

Practice documents can be obtained starting from Sunday, 14/09/2025, and on subsequent days during official working hours from the Procurement Department's website (https://pur.ku.edu.kw).

1- The deadline for submitting bids is Tuesday, 07/10/2025, at 12:00 PM. Bids received after this deadline will not be considered. Bids will be opened in a public session.

2- Instructions for Practitioners:
- Bids must be submitted via optical discs (CDs) (3 copies), ensuring that the copying process for all files has been completed correctly before depositing the discs in the submission envelope. The discs must be identical, similar, protected, and non-modifiable for the data, and each must contain all practice documents signed and sealed with the practitioner's (company's) stamp.
- Inquiries are accepted within 10 days from the date of the announcement. No inquiries will be accepted after the specified deadline.
- The following paper documents must be submitted:
    - The original copy of the bid form and undertaking.
    - Initial security (as per the tender announcement).
    - Purchase receipt from the website.
    - A copy of a valid and effective national labor percentage certificate.
    - A valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file.
    - The envelope designated for the practice.
- The bid will be disqualified if any document mentioned in the instructions is not submitted.
- Bids are to be placed in the designated box at the Procurement Department – in the University Administration Building (Al-Shaddadiya <orig>الشدادية</orig>) – Sixth Floor – Suppliers Affairs Section.
- Note: Practice documents are to be collected by companies specialized in this field, provided they are registered with the University's Suppliers Affairs Section and registered with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, during official working hours.

# General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig>
### Announcement
**Tender No. (12-2026/2025)**
**Supply of Printed Materials and Agendas**

The General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> announces a tender for the supply of printed materials and agendas, open to specialized companies and institutions in accordance with the general and special conditions stated in the tender documents.

Therefore, companies and institutions wishing to participate in this tender must register on the General Presidency of the National Guard's <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> website (www.kng.gov.kw) to purchase the tender documents for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only. Payment is to be made through the National Guard's website using the (K-NET) service.

A preliminary meeting will be held at 10:00 AM on Monday, 29/09/2025, at the General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig>, Colonel Staff / Faisal Al-Jareed <orig>فيصل الجريد</orig> Building. Whether the practitioner attends or not, they will be bound by all decisions, recommendations, or clarifications contained in this meeting. Participating companies and institutions must print the minutes of the preliminary meeting from the National Guard's website (www.kng.gov.kw). The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Wednesday, 15/10/2025.

These documents can be obtained from the headquarters of the National Fund for the Care and Development of Small and Medium-sized Enterprises <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> in Al Hamra Real Estate Tower <orig>برج الحمراء العقاري</orig> in Sharq area, Al-Shuhada Street <orig>شارع الشهداء</orig>, 63rd Floor, Procurement Department <orig>دائرة المشتريات</orig>, upon submission of an authorization letter to purchase the documents, a copy of the company's licenses and papers, and proof of the company's work in the field of the practice.

## Meeting Proceedings and Decisions
### Item One:
The minutes of the previous Committee meeting No. (2025/97) held on 31/8/2025 were approved.

### Item Two:
The attendance of the esteemed Committee members for the upcoming Committee meeting No. (2025/99) was recorded. A legal quorum for its convening was confirmed.

# Announcement

Announcement
Regarding the List of Companies Invited to Participate in
Limited Tender No. KPI-SS-21082025 for Providing a Travel Agency
for Kuwait Petroleum International's <orig>شركة البترول الكويتية العالمية</orig> Head Office
The Higher Procurement Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> for Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> tenders and its subsidiaries, upon the request of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>, announces the list of companies invited to participate in Limited Tender No. KPI-SS-21082025 for providing a travel agency for Kuwait Petroleum International's <orig>شركة البترول الكويتية العالمية</orig> Head Office.
In this regard, we draw attention to the fact that, based on the text of Article 16 of Law No. 49 of 2016 concerning Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>, the aforementioned tender will be offered to the following list of 14 companies at least 30 days from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>). Any interested party whose name is not included in the list of companies invited to the tender has the right to appeal their exclusion or submit a request to participate in the tender, supported by relevant documents, addressed to the Chairman of the Higher Procurement Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> for Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> tenders and its subsidiaries within 30 days from the date of publication of this announcement.
Furthermore, a fee of (250 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) will be collected from companies applying to participate, to be deposited into Kuwait Petroleum International's <orig>شركة البترول الكويتية العالمية</orig> account as specified below. The applicant must attach the payment receipt for the fees with their application, otherwise their application will be considered rejected.

- The last date for submitting bids is Thursday, 18/12/2025, at 1:00 PM local time for the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> (13:00 Noon), noting that bids must be submitted through the commercial electronic platform mentioned above.

Bids not accompanied by a payment receipt will be excluded. If the bid is submitted electronically, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid.
- It is noted that this is a general, indivisible tender, as the supply will be from the unified qualification list of the Central Qualification Committee <orig>لجنة التأهيل المركزية</orig> mentioned in the tender documents.
- No single person or group of persons acting together may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
- However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its own legal personality, finances, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies.
- A bidder's offer that violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law, in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>.
- It is noted that a preliminary remote meeting for bidders will be held (online) via Microsoft Teams application at 10:00 AM on Wednesday, 24/9/2025, to answer bidders' inquiries. The meeting link - and other details for joining the meeting - will be sent to all bidders through the company's Commercial Web Page (CWP), which bidders should regularly monitor for updates regarding the tender.

Note:
- All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the commercial electronic platform as specified in the tender documents.
- The Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> wishes to draw the attention of Messrs./Bidders who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical specifications to submit such requests a maximum of (two weeks) before the closing date (for this tender). These requests will be rejected and will not be considered for any reason whatsoever after this deadline.
- To obtain a username and password for accessing the commercial electronic platform, please contact phone numbers 23887794/23887792.
- Email: cwphelp@knpc.com
- Illustrative guidelines on how to submit a bid by visiting the commercial electronic platform are available on our website.

- A certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> and valid for one year, must be attached with the tender submission.
- Attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that there is no suspension of the tenderer's file from government contracts registered with the Authority due to any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 6 of 2010 regarding work in the private sector.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempt from the prescribed fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to submit a tender must attach with their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development and Care <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
- Any changes to the tender will be announced through the Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>كويت اليوم</orig> newspaper or via the commercial electronic page mentioned above.
- Companies wishing to participate in this tender, and for which the specifications and criteria required in the practice documents apply, must be registered on the Unified Commercial Electronic Platform (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
https://www.ktendering.com.kw → Supplier Registration → Fill in all the required details and submit the registration request
- To obtain a username and password for accessing the commercial electronic page, please contact +965-23898811 or via email (K-HELP@KIPIC.COM.KW).
- Illustrative guidelines on how to submit a bid through the commercial electronic page are available on our website.

- Based on the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 regarding Public Tenders: "No single person or group of persons combined may register under more than one name during classification or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may register himself and each of his independent companies during classification. Any bid from a tenderer violating this article shall be deemed null and void by judgment."
- The tenderer must deposit the bid form along with the original preliminary bond in an envelope marked with the tender name, address, and closing date, and place it in the designated bids box located at the company's headquarters - Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> Office Buildings Complex - Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig> - Gate No. (1) - Building (B1) - Ground Floor.
- All required documents, papers, and certificates must be submitted through the electronic system mentioned above and as specified in the tender documents.
- Please note that this is a general tender, divisible, and alternative bids are not permitted.
- The tenderer must deposit the tender document purchase fee into the Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> account mentioned below, with the necessity of adding the tender number and company name to the purchase receipt issued by the bank, and submitting the receipt with the bid. Bids not accompanied by a payment receipt will be excluded. If the bid is submitted electronically, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid:

### Announcement
Correction
Regarding Tender No.: 2151572-RFQ
BASKET STRAINERS
The Higher Purchasing Committee for tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries, upon the request of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>, wishes to draw the attention of the esteemed tenderers to the fact that the value of the preliminary bond for the aforementioned tender is K.D. 5,000/- and not as stated in the previous announcement published in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) Issue No. (1754), Page Nos. (238-237) dated 31/08/2025 regarding the aforementioned tender.
Hence, this notification is deemed necessary,
For any additional information, please visit the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> through the commercial electronic page (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:

## Announcement of Tender Invitation
No.: RFQ-2152690

The Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries, upon the request of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> - one of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation's <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> companies, announces the invitation for Tender No. RFQ-2152690
Tender Title: SUPPLY OF ESP FEED THROUGH PACKERS FOR SEK, NK & WK WELLS (WITH SERVICES)
in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the tender documents. These documents can be obtained through the e-Tendering Portal (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
https://www.ktendering.com.kw
RFQs/Tenders/Auctions (Open to all Suppliers) → Search for the RFP Title using the Filter.

- The bidder must deposit the bid form along with the original preliminary bond in an envelope marked with the name and address of the tender and the closing date, and place it in the designated bids box located at the company's headquarters – Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> Office Buildings Complex – Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig> – Gate No. (1) – Building (B1) – Ground Floor.
- All required documents, papers, and certificates must be submitted through the electronic system mentioned above and as specified in the tender documents.
- Please note that this is a general tender, indivisible, and alternative bids are not permitted.
- The bidder must deposit the tender document purchase fee into the Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> account mentioned below, with the necessity of adding the tender number and the company name to the purchase receipt issued by the bank, and submitting the receipt with the bid. Bids not accompanied by the payment receipt will be excluded. If the bid is submitted electronically, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid:

BANK NAME: NATIONAL BANK OF KUWAIT, AHMADI BRANCH
ACCOUNT NO.:1001058663
SWIFT CODE: NBOKKWKW
IBAN: KW77NBOK0000000000001001058663
ACCOUNT NAME: KUWAIT OIL COMPANY
OR
BANK NAME: GULF BANK, FAHAHEEL BRANCH, KUWAIT
ACCOUNT NO.:8801243
SWIFT CODE: GULBKWKW
IBAN: KW62GULB000000000000008801243
ACCOUNT NAME: KUWAIT OIL COMPANY
- Bidders wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must adhere to submitting them to the relevant party at the time and place specified above and according to the schedule for the preliminary meeting (inquiry session). (Not Applicable)
- The right to attend the preliminary meeting is restricted to bidders who have purchased the tender documents, with a maximum of two persons from each company, accompanied by a letter of authorization from the company and a copy of the tender document purchase receipt.
- The deadline for receiving inquiries and clarifications from companies is 17/11/2025, and no inquiries or clarifications received after this date will be considered.
- A certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> and valid for one year, must be attached with the bid.
- Attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that there is no suspension on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority due to any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 6 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector.
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises are exempt from the prescribed fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments

*   Any changes to tenders will be announced through Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> newspaper or via the commercial e-page mentioned above.
*   Companies wishing to participate in this tender, and for which the specifications and criteria required in the practice documents apply, must be registered on the Unified Commercial Electronic Platform (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
    `https://www.ktendering.com.kw`
    `→ Supplier Registration → Fill in all the required details and submit the registration request`
*   To obtain a username and password to access the commercial e-page, please contact +965-23898811 or via email: (K-HELP@KIPIC.COM.KW)
*   Illustrative guidelines on how to submit a bid through the commercial e-page are available on our website.

Announcement

### Annual Plan for Supply, Contracting, and Services Contracts

Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces that, in accordance with Article No. (33) and Article No. (88) of Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016 regarding the subject of the aforementioned announcement, plans are published weekly on the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>. Therefore, all those wishing to view them should visit the website continuously to get the latest updates by following these steps:
1- Company Website WWW.KOCKW.COM
2- Click on E-business
3- Select one of the options: Tenders (RFP's) and Purchases (RFQ's)
4- Click on Upcoming
